US Trade with China Greatly Reduced in the First Half of This Year 47

(Washington) The Department of Commerce released a report today stating that the total value of US trade with China in July of this year was US$2,251,000, while in July of last year it was US$6,861,000. In the first seven months of this year, the total value of US goods exported to China was US$24,919,000, while in the same period last year it was US$44,807,000. In July of this year, the value of US goods imported from China was US$6,262,000, while in July of last year it was US$4,004,000. In the first seven months of this year, the total value of US goods imported from China was US$36,602,000, while in the same period last year it was US$28,722,000. This year, US trade with the US is in a surplus position, which is actually caused by the US purchasing a large amount of silver from China. Furthermore, in the first half of last year, China purchased a total of 778,220 dan of cotton, of which 272,889 dan were purchased from the United States. In the same period this year, China purchased 405,263 dan of cotton, of which 200,460 dan were purchased from the United States. In the first half of last year, China purchased 17,665,000 kilograms of tobacco leaves from the US. In the same period this year, it only purchased 3,883,000 kilograms. (6th National News Agency)

(Washington) US trade with China has decreased. According to officials from the Department of Agriculture, this is actually due to the decline in China's purchasing power and the increase in China's domestic cotton production. It is found that the total cotton exports of all countries in the world in the first half of this year are only half of that in the same period last year, but the percentage occupied by the United States has not changed. As for the decline in tobacco exports, the reason is also the decline in China's purchasing power. In addition, Chinese tobacco merchants previously purchased too much stock when prices were low, which is also one of the reasons. As for wheat, the United States itself does not subsidize exports. There is no expectation for US trade with China before there is a major improvement in the domestic situation in China. (6th National News Agency)

(Washington) According to the Department of Commerce, the total value of silver imported into the United States in the week before August 30 was $3,116,000. In the previous week, it was $6,492,000. Among them, Mexico supplied $1,866,000, Canada supplied $521,000, Peru $193,000, and the United Kingdom $380,000. This time, no silver was purchased from China or Hong Kong. This figure shows that the high tide of US silver purchases has subsided, because the purchased silver is all from major silver producing countries. That is, the amount purchased is very small compared to the $14,604,000 imported in the week before August 9. The total value of silver exported this time reached $559,000, of which $500,000 was shipped to Honduras. (6th National News Agency)

(London) During the week ending September 4, British silver exports increased slightly compared to the previous week, while imports increased greatly. The total value of exports was £1,524,000, an increase of £50,000 compared to the previous week. The amount shipped to the United States this week was £1,515,000, an increase of £61,000 compared to the previous week. British silver imports this week were valued at £1,751,000, an increase of £1,164,000 compared to the previous week. The total value came from Japan was £322,000, Belgium £25,000, Hong Kong £1,259,000, France £44,000, India £21,000, and French Somaliland £20,000. This week's silver trade surplus was £127,000, while last week's surplus was £887,000. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Roosevelt Halts New Deal, Opinions Vary, A Prelude to the Presidential Election Campaign 48

(Washington) Opinions vary in commercial and political circles on the letters exchanged between President Roosevelt and H. L. Howard. Franklin, chairman of the Republican Central Committee, expressed his opinion that the president has issued new promises to begin the 1936 election campaign. Massachusetts Governor Curley praised the letter and predicted that Roosevelt would be re-elected. Senator Norris said that the letter was well-worded. After reading the letter, Chicago capitalist Rice Gower said, "If we praise this letter highly, we predict that Roosevelt will be re-elected. Senator Norris said that the letter was well-worded. After reading the letter, Chicago capitalist Rice Gower said, "From a spiritual point of view, this letter is important." Glaser, the manager of Otis Steel Company, said, "It is difficult to say whether the President's promise can compensate for past losses." (6th National News Agency)

(New York) Banks have a very good impression of President Roosevelt's letter to Howard discussing the New Deal, and they regard it as a symbol of its continued drift to the right. But we are willing to hear promises that can give us relief. This statement should help commerce." (6th National News Agency)

(New York) Wall Street attaches great importance to President Roosevelt's statement that his basic recovery program has been completed and that the business community now has a chance to breathe. The business community breathed a sigh of relief upon hearing this. However, some quarters said that what the business community needs is not only a chance to breathe, but also a balanced budget, reduced taxes, and lower living costs before there can be a real recovery. Few officials in Washington admit that Roosevelt is prepared to relinquish the temporary emergency powers granted to him by Congress in a short period of time. However, the figure in the business world said that Roosevelt's remarks were intended to create an atmosphere of trust before the 1936 election. The stock market showed a lively atmosphere after hearing Roosevelt's statistics. Many Democrats have expressed dissatisfaction that the ongoing rapid reforms have suddenly been suspended, but Republicans feel that this is still not thorough. Only by balancing the budget can there be hope for recovery. Knox, the media tycoon in Chicago who once campaigned as a Republican candidate for president, claimed that Roosevelt's remarks were just another promise and would only be important if they were reliable. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

The League of Nations Forms a Five-Nation Committee; Italy Suddenly Expresses Approval; Invokes Article Fifteen of the Covenant for Handling; Abyssinia Also Replaces Representative 49

(Geneva) Last night, during a League of Nations Council meeting, the heated speech of Abyssinian representative Professor Jidji caused the Italian representative Roja to angrily leave the session. This matter has now been resolved. The Abyssinian government agreed today to appoint Ambassador Hawariat, the Abyssinian ambassador to Paris, as the chief representative to the League of Nations meetings, with Professor Jidji as his deputy. It is said that this measure can satisfy Italy, as Italy opposed Jidji because he was not Abyssinian and disliked his sharp tongue. At the same time, a compromise has been reached regarding the formation of a five-person special committee to handle the Italo-Abyssinian dispute in accordance with Article Fifteen of the League of Nations Covenant. After being pressured by Britain and France, Italy no longer insists that the Italian side should also send a representative to join the committee. The committee is now composed of British representative Eden, French representative Laval, Spanish representative Madariaga, Polish representative Beck, and Turkish representative Aras. This afternoon, when the Council met, the Abyssinian representative entered the meeting, and the Italian representative Aloisi left in protest. The Council then appointed this five-person special committee. After that, the Council discussed matters unrelated to the Abyssinian case, and Aloisi returned to the meeting.

The special committee held a short meeting tonight, electing Madariaga as chairman and deciding to hold its first important meeting at 10:30 tomorrow morning. The procedures for today have not yet been finalized, but it is expected that Eden and Laval will be authorized to negotiate with Aloisi. However, the committee will of course need to contact both Italy and Abyssinia. It is widely believed that Italy is now prepared to accept the proposals put forward at the Paris conference as a basis for discussion, but it must be a starting point and not a final conclusion. (Reuters, 6th)

(Geneva) The Five-Nation Committee has earnestly appealed to both Italy and Abyssinia not to take actions that could jeopardize the success of the committee's mediation efforts. The committee then held a short meeting, attended by all five representatives. After the meeting, Laval immediately returned to Paris, presumably to confer with President Lebrun and other cabinet members. Laval is scheduled to return to Geneva on September 10th.

According to reliable sources, Mussolini has assured Laval that Italy will not resort to force while the Geneva talks are in progress. (Reuters, 7th)

(Paris) Yesterday's newspapers clearly expressed disappointment with the situation in Geneva. Now that the Five-Nation Committee has been established, the tone has become more optimistic. Le Matin's headline was "The Calming of the Storm," stating that while Italy's attitude is more moderate and no longer resolutely opposes the inclusion of Britain and France in the Five-Nation Committee, the dispute is still far from being resolved. Le Journal stated that the establishment of the Five-Nation Committee is the first victory for the international community, and this victory is due to the efforts of Prime Minister Laval. The Geneva correspondent of the French semi-official news agency stated that the British and French foreign ministries have been drafting new proposals for several weeks, which may resolve the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. The solutions contained therein are broadly similar to those governing the relationship between Britain and Iraq, and will be submitted to the Five-Nation Committee today by Laval and Eden. The relationship between Britain and Iraq is based on the following two principles: (1) Britain recognizes Iraq's independence and the sovereignty of its King; (2) Iraq recognizes Britain's right to station troops and participate in Iraq's army and police. If this approach can be adopted for Italo-Abyssinian relations, then the arbitrary border management laws discussed during the Paris tripartite talks may be merged. However, the correspondent warned that this plan can only be realized if the outbreak of war is prevented. (National News Agency, 7th)

Rumors of Another Meeting Between Britain, France, and Italy; The Italian Political World Embraces This Hope 50

(Paris) Rome is rather pessimistic about the efforts of the Five-Nation Special Committee appointed by the League of Nations Council. Paris is now considering a plan to hold a new meeting between Britain, France, and Italy to replace it. According to Le Temps, the new meeting may still be held in Stresa. In April of this year, the three countries met there after Germany rearmed to discuss the policies to be pursued in Europe. The newspaper also stated that if the current plan can be realized, Mussolini wants Britain to be represented by Baldwin and Hoare, and France by Laval. L'Observateur in Paris believes that the Italo-Abyssinian dispute may be resolved through a human solution, allowing Italy to occupy a position in Abyssinia, as Britain does in Iraq. It is said that Italy will implement Abyssinia's police and administrative affairs, while Abyssinia will remain a member of the League of Nations. It is also said that Mussolini has sent a large army to East Africa, which can be used to conquer the border provinces that refuse to agree to this solution, so as to avoid the army being idle. (Reuters, 7th)

(Rome) Political figures have not abandoned hope of resolving the Abyssinian affair, but believe that the various plans currently being discussed in Geneva cannot be accepted. The hope for a final resolution lies in informal talks between the countries concerned, as this kind of informal talk often produces effective results, which is generally recognized. The main problem at present lies in the principles on which the various proposals put forward so far are based. One of these principles advocates that Britain, France, and Italy, together with Abyssinia, should jointly conclude a treaty in order to seek a thorough solution. However, Italian political figures believe that if this principle is agreed to, it will be a step backward compared to the 1906 tripartite treaty, which demarcated the spheres of influence of Britain, France, and Italy in Abyssinia without consulting Abyssinia beforehand. Now, it is desired to have Abyssinia conclude a treaty jointly with Britain, France, and Italy, which is naturally difficult for Italy to accept. In addition, political figures stated that what Italy is asking for is to govern the entire territory of Abyssinia, similar to Britain's governance of the African mandated territory of Tanganyika. However, this has not been accepted by all parties so far. In any case, the possibility of reaching an agreement outside the League of Nations mechanism has not disappeared. It is generally believed that it would be easier to reach an agreement if the foreign affairs officials of the countries concerned were to negotiate directly. If Italian Foreign Minister Mussolini, French Foreign Minister Laval, and British Foreign Secretary Hoare could meet together, it would be very helpful in resolving this issue. Therefore, political figures generally believe that the Stresa conference format may be adopted again. (Havas, 6th)

(London) According to well-informed sources, Britain's attitude towards the Abyssinian affair is based on the following three wishes: (1) to give Italy the opportunity to boost its prestige in Abyssinia and obtain psychological satisfaction in the short term; (2) to impose sanctions on Italy at the request of British public opinion, but not to have Italy regard these sanctions as an act of war; (3) to uphold the principles of the League of Nations. These are the wishes recently expressed by London financial circles, and it seems that responsible parties have also adopted this view. Therefore, the fact that Prime Minister Baldwin first received Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain yesterday is noteworthy. It is believed that if Britain and Italy were to clash, the damage to the world economy and the British economy would be significant. It is said that for the sake of Italy's prestige, Italy's expedition to Abyssinia is inevitable. Therefore, it is advocated that if Italian troops attack Adowa in Abyssinia, most of the Abyssinian troops should retreat to avoid a large-scale conflict with the Italian army. Once the Italian army wins a great victory, it can then carry out police-like actions within Abyssinia without engaging in a real war. As for the issue of sanctions, if Britain only prohibits the shipment of arms to Italy or allows the shipment of arms to Abyssinia, Italy may not immediately regard it as an act of war. If so, then after the Italian army wins a great victory at Adowa, wiping out the shame of 1896 and greatly enhancing its prestige, it will not be difficult for Britain to negotiate directly with Mussolini to finalize the matter. In addition, Foreign Secretary Hoare will go to Geneva to attend the 16th General Assembly of the League of Nations. Political figures are eagerly hoping for Hoare's speech at the General Assembly of the League of Nations, because this speech will surely shed new light on the Abyssinian issue. (Havas, 6th)

(Paris) French Senator Dumont expressed his opinion in the Economic News, advocating that the world's colonies should be reconsidered and redistributed. This proposal has now aroused heated discussions among prominent figures in Britain and the United States. Dumont first stated that the Kellogg-Briand Pact has stipulated that countries should not resort to war over the struggle for raw materials, but it is almost impossible to prevent countries with high birth rates and limited raw material resources from risking war. However, according to Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant, this issue really needs to be considered, that is, whether the current distribution of colonies, with some having too much and others having too little, is reasonable. (National News Agency, 6th)

(Paris) French newspapers today published editorials, stating that the opinions of the representatives in Geneva are consistent, and that Britain and France are now becoming increasingly united. Several newspapers warned the Italian government that it would be futile to confront the united and determined League of Nations alone. Le Petit Parisien stated that Italy should realize that the League of Nations is still a vigorous organization, and that the great powers are determined to respect international law, no matter how great the price. L'Écho de Paris believes that the status of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute has changed very little, but stated that it is now extremely obvious that Laval has abandoned his role as mediator and is leaning towards Britain. If so, then Italy's claims will inevitably be hit hard. (Reuters, 7th)

The Abyssinian Emperor Says Maintaining Peace Must Not Sacrifice Sovereignty; Hasty Arbitration Does Not Help the Overall Situation 51

(Paris) The Abyssinian government issued a lengthy statement yesterday criticizing the decision of the Italo-Abyssinian Mediation Committee, stating that the Walwal incident has now been resolved. This incident caused the current Italo-Abyssinian dispute and Italy's military preparations, but the Italo-Abyssinian problem remains because Italy refuses to seek reconciliation in accordance with the treaty. Since Abyssinia is a member of the League of Nations, it requests the League of Nations to abide by the resolution of August 4 this year, to adopt methods to resolve all disputes, to maintain peace, and not to adopt important principles that undermine the independence, sovereignty, and territorial integrity of members. It is Italy that is hindering the demarcation of the border between Somalia and Abyssinia. (National News Agency, 6th)

Italy Decides to Withdraw Consuls from Various Parts of Abyssinia; People in the Abyssinian Capital View This as an Ominous Sign 52

Addis Ababa The Italian envoy to Abyssinia informed the Abyssinian Foreign Ministry today that the Italian government has decided to withdraw its consuls stationed in various parts of Abyssinia, except for those in Harar and Adowa. People in the Abyssinian capital view this as a serious sign. It is estimated that a total of four consulates will be closed, and all consulate staff will come to the Abyssinian capital. (Reuters, 7th)

Naples A steamship carrying a batch of armaments and 300 vehicles set sail from here yesterday afternoon to the Italian port of Massawa in East Africa. Another ship, carrying military supplies and fodder, followed it to the same destination. When this ship set sail, it was discovered that about 30 young men were hiding in the cargo hold, hoping to secretly go to East Africa to serve the country. The ship's owner sent them ashore and handed them over to their families to take them back. (Havas, 7th)

(Berlin) The North German Lloyd Shipping Company announced today that it has sold four of its ships, totaling 40,000 tons, to Italy. (National News Agency, 6th)

At the same time, representatives of various parties held a meeting at the League of Nations Association here, passing a resolution advocating that the government should take concerted action in Geneva with countries that maintain the League of Nations Covenant, and that the Council of the League of Nations should be requested to implement the League of Nations Covenant and not hesitate to impose sanctions on aggressor countries. (National News Agency, 7th)

The Policies of the British Dominions Are Quite Inconsistent; Canada Advocates Absolute Peace 57

London The official is very concerned about what kind of reaction the British dominions have to the implementation of sanctions when Italy attacks Abyssinia. In particular, the British government is paying close attention to the recent resolution passed by the Pretoria Chamber of Commerce, the capital of the Union of South Africa, requesting the government to protect the status quo of African territory. As far as the current situation is concerned, the attitudes of the British dominions can be roughly described as follows:

(1) Canada Canadian Prime Minister Bennett recently declared that the Canadian government's responsibility lies in preventing Canada from being drawn into the vortex of international disputes. However, Bennett's declaration may not have any effect, because the current Conservative government of Canada may soon be overthrown, and the claims of Liberal Party leader Mackenzie King are diametrically opposed to Bennett's. As for Canada's general public opinion, it does not seem to object to implementing sanctions and strengthening the effectiveness of the League of Nations Covenant.

(2) Australia Australian public opinion is not as divided on the Italo-Abyssinian issue as the other dominions. Australian Conservative Prime Minister Lyons and Social Democratic former Prime Minister Lang both oppose sanctions. However, the Australian Cabinet recently decided to support the British government's Geneva policy as much as possible. In addition, Australian public opinion generally supports maintaining the effectiveness of the League of Nations Covenant, but does not support the implementation of sanctions, because it fears that it will lead to war.

(3) Union of South Africa The three states of the Union of South Africa are all in full agreement with the strict implementation of the League of Nations Covenant, for three reasons: first, it fears that it will cause racial conflict in Africa. The conflict between colored and white people in Africa has been painstakingly eliminated, and it should not be allowed to revive now; second, because South Africans believe that fulfilling international obligations is morally very important; third, because of anti-fascist demonstrations by the South African labor class. The recent strike by South African dockworkers to refuse to load meat and ship it to East Africa to supply Italian troops is one example.

(4) New Zealand and Newfoundland These two regions will always support British policy, regardless of what it is.

It can be seen that the attitudes of the British dominions are quite different, but the British government will probably act alone and will not take into account the opinions of the various dominions, because the Italo-Abyssinian dispute is more important to Europe and has little to do with the entire British Empire. (Havas, 7th)

Ottawa Canadian Prime Minister Bennett made a broadcast speech tonight. While engaged in the federal election campaign, he declared that dangers are imminent, but the fault lies with others, not with us. I feel that the government should use all fair and honorable means to keep Canada out of it. This is the government's solemn responsibility. Canada knows very well the dangers of the international situation. In world politics, Canada should focus on security, because Canada has no ambition that peace cannot hope for. Canada has paid the price for safety and peace and has purchased it. We must now keep it from being lost. We should stay away from any foreign disputes that do not involve Canada's rights. (Reuters, 7th)

Once the reserve is fully established, it will be allocated 60% to local currency and 40% to post-reorganization public bonds. Jiangsu Province Abolishes Excessive and Miscellaneous Taxes - The Fourth Batch Still Has a Portion - To Be Implemented Once Funds Are Allocated by the Ministry 82

Zhenjiang Report: Jiangsu Province has previously abolished three batches of local excessive and miscellaneous taxes in various counties, totaling over 328,000 yuan annually. Now, for the fourth batch of taxes to be abolished, the Finance Department has sent a letter to the Jiangsu Province Tax Supervision Bureau, forwarding the survey registers from 48 counties to the department for review. It is estimated that over 590,000 yuan have already been automatically abolished in the fourth batch. Together with the previous three batches, this amounts to over 900,000 yuan, accounting for 80% of the originally planned total abolition amount. Furthermore, offsetting measures have been incorporated into the review of county budgets and the streamlining of financial plans, effectively tightening expenditures or finding ways to consolidate revenues. Without waiting for the central government to allocate subsidies, the burden on the people has been reduced. The remaining 190,000 yuan of the fourth batch of taxes to be abolished cannot be offset, and the Ministry of Finance has been requested to allocate the required amount from the stamp tax revenue. Implementation can commence once the Ministry allocates the funds. As for the remaining twelve counties, further review and abolition will be carried out after the Tax Supervision Bureau completes its survey.

International Commercial Telegrams 83

- Reuters Special Commercial Telegram, September 7 -

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 141 shillings and 1 penny, 3 pence higher than yesterday.

London Silver Market: Sales were light this morning, with a slight increase in prices. Spot and futures both rose .0625, reaching 29 pence and .25. India and China made purchases, while China and speculators sold. The market closed steadily.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market, the pound sterling continued to be sold this morning. The French franc was subject to regulation by the Exchange Equalisation Fund. The opening exchange rate for British-American was $4.92875, which was one-half cent lower than the closing rate of American-British yesterday. It rose .0625 in the first hour and remained unchanged afterward. It rose another .0625 at the close.

British-French: The opening price fell by two pounds sterling to 74 francs and 85 centimes. It fell by three pounds sterling in the first hour and by four pounds sterling at the close, reaching 74 francs and 78 centimes.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened mixed today (7th). The October contract rose by four points, but the May contract fell by three points. The market continued to be volatile. Market participants are awaiting the government estimate to be released on Monday, with generally mixed expectations.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was quiet. The closing price for the October contract was 5.65, down one point.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market surged today due to a sudden increase in Canadian wheat prices. The closing price for the October contract was 5 shillings and 1 and 3/8 pence, up one and a half pence.

American Wheat: The Canadian government set a minimum wheat price of 87.5 cents, which strengthened the Chicago wheat market today. The opening price was 1.625 cents higher, with very active trading. Shortly thereafter, the price rose another 1.625 cents, but profit-taking led to a fall of .375. This drop was brief, and the recent market price rose again by .125. Grains followed the wheat market, opening .625 higher and then rising another half cent, but prices plummeted due to profit-taking.

Rubber

London: The market was very quiet today, with the January-March period falling by .025. At noon, it returned to yesterday's closing price of 5 pence and .6875.

New York: The opening price fell by seven points and then returned to yesterday's closing price. Trading was very light.

Securities

New York: President Roosevelt's remarks that basic recovery had been completed and that the business community now needed time to breathe have attracted significant attention in the New York securities market. The active trading before yesterday's close reappeared this morning, and the prices of various securities rose across the board. US Steel rose by one point. Utilities were slightly higher but not as firm as other stocks. The Dow Jones average of thirty industrial stocks opened at 131.09, up thirty-four points. Impressions of a Southern Tour 84

— Special Correspondent Qian Hua

(33) The Issue of Women's Military Training

The women of Guangdong and Guangxi are the bravest and most active. Traveling west from Guangzhou into Guangxi, the active state of the working women seen along the way becomes more and more pronounced. Most of the women in Guangxi Province have considerable occupations, and their ability to handle affairs is almost completely equal to that of men, or even surpasses it. All agencies and schools have female staff, dressed in men's clothing, wearing ordinary gray cloth uniforms, and military caps, with the spirit of warriors. Middle schools and elementary schools are co-educational, and men and women swim in the same swimming pool. The authorities are extremely open-minded, and no adverse incidents have been discovered. In rural areas, men and women are even more equal. Both sides operate in the same way. The reporter traveled more than 5,000 miles back and forth on various highways by car. In the villages passed, women carrying babies on their backs, shouldering loads weighing more than a hundred catties, wearing large bamboo hats, black shirts and trousers, barefoot, and straw sandals were everywhere. Fifteen- or sixteen-year-old girls, barefoot, were carrying water, herding cattle, or transplanting rice seedlings, as active as boys. It is said that men in Guangxi are lazy and indulge in gambling, often losing everything they earn in one throw. The wives, on the other hand, are frugal and thrifty, holding the economic power of the family. Jokers say that they can afford to keep three wives and four concubines, distribute them to seek food and work, while they themselves sit back and direct, and in a few years, they can become wealthy and harmful old men. Hence, the occupation of women in Guangxi is entirely based on labor skills to obtain remuneration, unlike women in certain provinces who are heavily made up and dressed up, only to be criticized as mere vases. Guangxi can truly implement gender equality. Since the environment for men and women in Guangxi is based on this truly equal principle, since the implementation of universal military training, the regulations stipulate that women should be trained in first aid techniques due to their physical strength and special physiological characteristics, but most female students above the middle school level have volunteered to undergo military training. The school authorities praised their aspirations and allowed them to join. The reporter visited Mr. Liang Hansong, commander of the militia district. Mr. Liang said that when the first phase of military training was held, many women asked to participate. Their reason was that men and women each account for half of the country. In the past, women's demands for participation in political power were all false because women did not participate in military affairs and economy. How could they participate in politics? Therefore, they first requested to participate in military training and share the hardships with men, and then they would have the opportunity to participate in politics. What he said was very true. Therefore, the authorities decided that starting next year, they would officially allow women to participate in military training and be treated the same as men. After completing training at the Militia Cadre School, they can be assigned as village chiefs and principals of elementary schools, and then gradually promoted according to qualifications and merits. That is to say, female village chiefs, county magistrates, and other local officials will soon be commonly seen in Guangxi.

(34) Conditions in Villages and Townships with Militias

Those who visited the militia command of the Wuming-Nanning District included, in addition to the reporter, legislators Wang Kunlun and Lin Suyuan, and several academic members. They had lunch at the district headquarters. After the meal, Commander Liang accompanied them on a tour of the various buildings in the headquarters for a week, including improved livestock farms, stables, houses for cattle, pigs, chickens, ducks, etc., which were extremely clean, as well as agricultural experimental fields, where various fruits and trees were planted. The large playground, hospital, and education room occupied a vast area. In addition to training militia cadre personnel, it also taught farmers attached to the area to improve agricultural work. Then, they took cars to visit the lower-level militia situation in the nearby Chaojie Village. The entire village had only dozens of households. The village office was located at the site of an old land temple, which had been slightly repaired and rebuilt. It was attached to a national basic elementary school with more than 20 students. The village chief and principal was a young man in his twenties. He converted the old land hall into a living room with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen hanging above it. On both walls were charts showing the number of households and educated people. Another chart detailed the amount of public property in the entire village, such as rural warehouses, village forests, village fields, village farmlands, public houses, village orchards, and other items, with detailed figures below each. According to Mr. Liang, the village warehouses, etc., belong to the public property of the entire village, so that the strength of group cooperation can be used to develop the rural economy and implement the militia's rural self-sufficiency policy. Regarding village fields, orchards, etc., the cultivation and management work is entirely a voluntary labor system. For example, each person contributes two workdays per month. With 300 people in the whole village, there are 600 workdays per month. All farmers aged 18 to 50 must respond to the call. In the future, the harvest of agricultural products will be included in the rural public warehouse. The village chief's salary is only 10 to 15 yuan per month, and they can be re-elected for two years. It is also stipulated that a certain percentage of the prosperity of the public warehouse will be used as a reward for the village chief's efforts, so their lives are still sufficient to maintain, and they can do their best to develop public interests, etc. Most of the people in the village have the surname Lu, and the village chief is also named Lu. To the right of the village office is a public entertainment place, which was also rebuilt from a temple. According to the village chief, the temple idols in various villages have been cleared one after another. At first, the village women complained about worshiping idols, but after explanation, they were able to understand. When the militia was first established, many villagers were also skeptical and watched, but after the village chiefs and others set an example, they now know that the militia is beneficial to the farmers themselves and actively participate, etc. After leaving Zhaojie Village, they went to nearby villages along the road. They saw militiamen with guns standing guard, brave and strong, in high spirits, washing away the shame of the "Sick Man of East Asia." Finally, they went to Wenjiang Pagoda, which was built during the Daoguang period of the Qing Dynasty. Located in the center of nearby villages, the militia lookout post was placed on the highest level of the pagoda. Before we left the command, Commander Liang had ordered the cannons to be fired to gather the militia for exercises. When we climbed the lookout tower to look out, militiamen were heading in teams on various roads from afar and had already gathered in the square. We also rushed over. The field could accommodate tens of thousands of people and was a natural training ground. A mat shed was erected in the middle as a command post. About a thousand militiamen were concentrated, and the team was very prosperous. Then the guests, at the invitation of Commander Liang, gave speeches in succession, mostly encouraging. At about 3 o'clock, the reporters and others left with satisfaction. On the way back, we saw militiamen working in groups of three or five, doing voluntary work, either building roads or planting, diligently working, it can be said that they are truly working for the public good.

(35) General Overview of Border Militias

Longzhou is the center of border defense. Initially, there was a stationed division. Since the establishment of the militia, universal military training has been gradually completed in the countryside, and the border defense has become more stable. The stationed army has been transferred to Bose in batches to prevent and suppress border communists. Only two regiments are currently stationed in Longzhou. Li Pinxian, the border defense supervisor and simultaneous anti-corruption supervisor, also serves as the commander of the Longzhou District Militia, the principal of the Republic Cadre School, and the administrative supervisor. Regarding the situation of the border defense militia, Mr. Li told the reporter that the regular teams in various counties have been established since 1931. The training period for each term is six months. After the term expires, they are discharged from the army. All books, pens, ink, and paper are prepared by the soldiers of each regiment themselves. In addition to regular classes, they are also made to learn planting, animal husbandry, gardening, and other things, in order to cultivate their production skills. After the training period expires, personnel are sent to inspect and fill in the scores of each subject, and a certificate is issued upon application. Those who fail must make up their studies for a certain period of time. After graduation, they are assigned to the reserve team. The standing team was discontinued in October 1933. From the beginning of the establishment to the end, a total of three terms were trained, and the number of discharged personnel was more than 3,740. The reserve team was established in 1932. The training period was initially 120 hours, and later increased to 180 hours with the addition of air defense, poison gas defense, and fire prevention. Due to geographical and soldier living conditions, the time can be changed as appropriate, but it must deduct a full 180 hours of training and not hinder the people's livelihood. After the term expires, personnel are sent to inspect, and those who pass are issued certificates. From July to December 1932, the first term was trained. From January to June 1933, the second term was trained. From July to December 1933, the third term was trained. From March to August 1934, the fourth term of the urban area was trained. From September 1934 to February 1935, the fourth term of the rural area was trained. From March 1935 to the present, the fifth term has been trained. Up to the fourth term, each county has trained a total of 338 reserve teams, with a total of 32,799 soldiers. After the standing team was discontinued, the original funds were changed to run a cadre training brigade. The number of personnel is the same as that of the standing team. The purpose is to train lower-level cadres of the Republic by slightly adjusting the incumbent village chiefs and other personnel to the team. The training period is eight months. After graduation, they return to serve as village chiefs and simultaneously serve as the reserve team leader, elementary school principal, or teacher. Up to the fourth term last year, the number of village chiefs in the Longzhou District who received training totaled 1,402, of which 1,029 have graduated. The Longzhou District Militia Cadre School was also established this spring. Incumbent village chiefs and graduates of Longzhou Middle School are sent to receive training. Longzhou is surrounded by mountains, sparsely populated, and close to the tropics, with rampant malaria. In recent years, transportation has gradually become more convenient, and roads on various lines have been completed one after another. It takes eight hours to reach Longzhou from Nanning by car along the highway. By water, it takes two or three days in high water and seven or eight days in shallow water. For aviation, there is the Guangzhou-Longzhou line, which flies from Guangzhou via Wuzhou and Nanning to Longzhou and can be reached in one day, making travel convenient. Merchants are also gradually converging. Guangxi Province pays great attention to health and administrative construction, and sends personnel to Longzhou to conduct research and treatment. Epidemics have been greatly reduced. It will further encourage immigration. On the one hand, due to the successful organization of the militia, bandits have disappeared, and people live and work in peace and contentment. Therefore, the future development of the Longzhou District can be predicted, and border defense should also be consolidated.

The Match Industry in Guangdong Province is Declining - Imported Matches are Dumped in the Mainland - Guangdong Manufacturers Request Suspension of the Consolidated Tax 85

Guangzhou Correspondence: The match industry in Guangdong Province once prospered, but later, imported matches were dumped, and the made-in-Guangdong matches were greatly affected. Initially, the match market in Southeast Asia was crowded out by foreign matches, and sales were cut off. Gradually, the place where matches were manufactured in this province was also invaded by foreign matches. As a result, Guangdong match factories were hit hard and closed down one after another. From hundreds of factories, there are more than ten factories left. To this day, their business is still sluggish and they are on the verge of self-preservation. Match merchants convened meetings on August 26 and 30 to request the Guangdong, Fujian, and Guangxi Consolidated Tax Bureau to exempt the consolidated tax on matches and simultaneously request the tax bureau to order inspectors to strictly investigate privately imported foreign matches to prevent the dumping of foreign goods. At the last collective discussion, the Consolidated Tax Bureau put forward its opinion that foreign matches are sold for only more than three yuan per piece, while domestically produced matches are sold for about ten yuan per piece. Even if more than four yuan and five angles per piece are removed from the consolidated tax and raw material tax, the price of domestically produced matches is still no match for the cheap price of imported matches. It is hoped that the match merchants in this province will fundamentally improve their work, so as to reduce costs. On the one hand, the government should appropriately reduce the consolidated tax in order to compete with foreign products. As for the methods of improving the match industry, there are about a number of points: (1) Rationalize the organization and management of match factories, (2) Rationalize the work of match factories, (3) Improve production technology, (4) Modernize mechanical equipment, (5) Improve the quality of local matches, with the standard of being better than foreign matches, (6) Implement production and sales cooperation, (7) Study the most economical means of purchasing raw materials, (8) Ensure that both labor and management stabilize the business, (9) Improve the knowledge and skills of laborers and their treatment. As a result, match merchants agreed to accept the business improvement plan, but since the current consolidated tax on matches is hindering the vitality of matches made in this province, they requested that the tax be suspended first in order to support the declining industry. The Director of the Consolidated Tax Bureau immediately replied that he would ask his superiors to consider it.

The Anhui Finance Department is Preparing to Establish a Local Bank - Joint Stock Investment is Solicited, and the Organization is in Accordance with Company Regulations - 86

Anqing Correspondence: Anhui Province has suffered frequent floods and droughts in recent years, as well as banditry. The government's treasury is depleted and difficult to replenish, while the rural areas are declining and industry and commerce are withering. The reason for this is that funds are concentrated in cities, and inland finance is completely stagnant. The only way to remedy this is to rely on an agency that can regulate finance, so that it can be operated flexibly. The Finance Department believes that the establishment of a provincial local bank is the most important plan at present, and in order to unify the collection and payment of various funds in the province and counties, it has planned to establish county treasuries in various counties. This county treasury should also be entrusted to local banks to act as agents nearby. Therefore, it is planned to prepare for the establishment of the Anhui Provincial Local Bank, solicit joint stock investment, and organize it in accordance with company regulations. The main significance of this is described below: (A) Positive aspects: (1) Rescue rural areas, (2) Support all industries and commerce, (3) Act as a treasury to unify revenue and expenditure, (4) Assist in production and construction and other production undertakings, (B) Negative aspects: Absolutely do not use it for political expenses. Based on the above significance, it is planned to complete the organization and actively proceed at the beginning of this year, so that the economic panic in this province can be directly and effectively assisted, and the effectiveness of politics can be improved, and the stability of social order can be relied upon. The key points for handling the agency treasury have been stipulated: A. In order to implement the treasury system in this province, the method of entrusting the bank to act as an agent will be adopted. Provincial treasuries and county treasuries will be established in the places where the provincial government and county governments are located to manage the revenue and expenditure of provincial and county funds. B. The provincial treasury will be entrusted by the provincial government to the bank located in the place to act as its agent. The county treasury will be entrusted by the county government to the bank branch or agency established by the bank acting as the agent of the provincial treasury. C. From the date of being entrusted, the bank branch or agency acting as the agent of the county treasury will collect and pay all provincial and county annual revenues and expenditures, except as otherwise provided by laws, regulations, or contracts. D. The bank branch or agency acting as the agent of the provincial and county treasuries shall store the treasury funds separately from the operating capital, but with the approval of the provincial financial authorities and the county government, a part of the treasury funds may be transferred to deposits, and the deposit interest shall be agreed upon by the bank branch or agency and the financial department and county government. E. The revenue and expenditure of special accounting, except as otherwise provided by laws and regulations, will also be managed by the acting provincial and county treasuries, and boundaries must be drawn to prevent mixing with operating capital revenue and expenditure. F. The Finance Department may send personnel at any time to inspect the provincial and county treasury disaster registers and cash, and the county governments of each county may also send personnel to inspect the county treasury disaster registers and cash on an ad hoc basis. (September 4)

Fengxian: Incest, Abortion, Widow Dies 87

Wuxi: Continued Appeal for Wheat Business Tax 88

The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce, based on the previous joint telegram from the flour and rice/bean industries to the ministry and provincial authorities requesting exemption from the temporary business tax on barley, received a reply from the Ministry of Finance yesterday. The reply stated that business tax collected by brokers should be levied from the seller. Flour factories purchasing wheat should be responsible for ensuring that the grain merchants entrusted with the purchase collect and pay the relevant business tax. If the grain merchants use their own capital to buy and sell grain, their own business activities should be subject to business tax. If the manufacturers entrust the purchase to grain merchants, the grain merchants should still be responsible for paying the tax. As for the method of tax collection by brokers, reforms have already been consulted and recorded. If grain brokers who handle buying and selling for customers collect commissions, they should still collect the tax from the seller according to the ministry's previous consultations. The buyer, whether a manufacturer or not, should not be taxed. Upon receiving the telegram, the Chamber of Commerce immediately notified the relevant parties. However, they replied that flour factories buying wheat are not subject to business tax. Rice and bean grain merchants are acting as agents for customers and are already paying a brokerage license fee and a separate business tax. According to Article 10 of the Business Tax Law, the original brokerage tax can be converted to business tax at the original tax rate. Now, the grain merchants in Wuxi are paying both brokerage and business tax, which is an extra burden. If they are also required to collect the temporary business tax on wheat, although it is nominally collected from the seller, it is actually paid by the grain merchants. This contradicts Article 9 of the Business Tax Law, which requires the taxpayer to pay the tax directly. Customers also have an excuse, making it difficult to collect the tax. Given the current slump in the grain market and the approaching Mid-Autumn Festival, the local commercial situation is already precarious. Grain merchants are paying both brokerage and business tax, and customers are still requesting exemption. Therefore, they have again telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, continuing to appeal for the immediate suspension of the tax to stabilize the commercial market, after consulting with the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Furthermore, the flour factories have declared that, starting from the first of this month, they will directly purchase wheat from the producers and will no longer buy and sell through brokers. However, the rice and bean businesses, because the grain merchants have paid the brokerage license fee, are bound by the regulations regarding measuring tools and cannot operate freely, leading to a stalemate. Therefore, no wheat grains have been purchased in the past week.

Xiaoming Case: Exhumation for Examination 89

In the area of Xiaoyuan Village near Zhouxin Town in the third district of the county, Zhou Tianrong, the four-year-old beloved son of Zhou Hexi, a resident, was allegedly poisoned by Zhou Gu, his great-grandmother by adoption. They arrived in Zhenru at noon. At 2 p.m., the coffin was opened for examination. Tianrong's body had not yet decomposed. His heart, liver, lungs, intestines, kidneys, and other organs were removed for chemical analysis. The coffin was first transported to Wuxi, where Prosecutor Shen will hold a court session and instruct Zhou Hexi, the father, to claim the body for burial. The results of the chemical analysis will be sent by the institute to the court for handling.

Haimen: Ministry of Communications Thoroughly Investigates Monopoly of Shipping 91

There were originally seven commercial ships operating between Shanghai and Haimen: Guangxiang, Baofeng, Baohua, Daxing, Fuxing, Haimen, and Xinrenhe. This spring, the shipping companies jointly organized the Shanghai-Haimen Shipping Cooperative, operating only two ships per shift, in order to monopolize business and raise ticket and freight prices, resulting in overcrowded passengers and goods. Fresh goods such as fruits and fish often rotted due to delayed loading and transportation, causing significant losses to merchants and travelers. The various trade associations in the county jointly petitioned the Ministry of Communications to strictly ban this practice. After receiving the petition, the Ministry of Communications ordered Sun Yongyi, the chief inspector of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, to come to Haimen to investigate (on the 3rd). That afternoon, he convened a meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce with the chairmen of various trade associations. Sun expressed dissatisfaction with the shipping companies' monopolistic practices. On the afternoon of the 5th, Sun returned to Shanghai by ship from Niuhong Port to report the results of the investigation to the Ministry of Communications for review.

Ningbo: Murder and Robbery Incidents Occur in Fenghua and Xiangshan 94

In Yaojia, Tingxia Dong Village, in the third district of Fenghua, most of the residents are farmers. Yao Zongshan, a farmer, has always been diligent and frugal and has saved a little money. In August of the 19th year, he was once kidnapped by thieves but managed to escape, avoiding losses. His wife, Zhang, has two daughters and one son. The son is only one year old. Because the second daughter is about to get married, the eldest daughter, who has already married, was brought back to help with everything. Unexpectedly, at 9 o'clock the night before last, six or seven bandits suddenly arrived, each holding firearms and other weapons. At that time, his wife, Zhang, and eldest daughter were silenced by the thieves and forbidden to make any noise. The bandit saw his young son sleeping on the bed and kidnapped him. The mother and daughter saw their son being kidnapped and grabbed him, refusing to let go, which angered the thieves. They opened fire and shot him dead. The bandits, realizing that they had caused trouble, tried to escape, but were stopped by the second daughter, who was also shot and injured by the bandits. The bullet is still in her abdomen. At the same time, Zhu Qianyun, a neighbor, heard the news and reported a fire to ask for help. He was also shot in the buttocks by the bandits. The thieves then kidnapped the hostage and fled towards Siming Bridge. Afterward, Zongshan returned home and saw his wife and eldest daughter had died tragically, his second daughter and neighbor were injured, and his beloved son was kidnapped. He was in extreme pain. Later, he found a letter left by the bandits in the house, demanding 8,550 yuan as ransom and specifying the address and date for the ransom payment. Zongshan immediately took the letter and reported it to the Dongcun Security Corps to pursue the bandits. Because so much time had passed, the bandits had already fled far away.

Jiangxi Finance Director Wu Jiantao Consults with Banking Industry on Grain Loans; Visited Minister Kong Yesterday to Request Instructions and Report Everything; Satisfactory Results; Returned to Xunzhou from Shanghai Last Night 98

According to Shen Shi News Agency, Wu Jiantao, the Director of Finance of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, came to Shanghai from Jiangxi a few days ago to contact the Shanghai banking industry for grain loans for Jiangxi Province to help the rural areas. He left at 12:45.

Grain Loans

According to Wu, who spoke to the Shen Shi News Agency reporter yesterday, "My visit to Shanghai this time is to contact the Shanghai banking industry for grain loans and to ask for assistance from various banks. This year's grain production in Jiangxi Province, except for northern Jiangxi, which was affected by floods and had a slight reduction in harvest, the agricultural affairs in other counties in southern Jiangxi and in the former bandit areas have been bountiful. The amount of grain produced is rare in recent decades. However, Jiangxi's rural economy has declined in the past due to bandit disasters. This year's grain harvest is so abundant that prices are bound to fall, which will greatly affect the livelihoods of farmers. Since his mission in Shanghai has been completed,　he returned to Jiangxi by China Merchants Bureau ship last night to report to Chairman Xiong. If necessary, Wu will come to Shanghai again in the next few days.

The memorial service for Queen Astrid of Belgium was held at the Catholic Church on Catholic Church Street yesterday morning at 11:00 a.m. The ceremony was solemn and respectful. Details are as follows:

At exactly 11:00 a.m., after Guillaume took his seat, the ceremony began. The Belgian national anthem was sung first, followed by mournful music. Loan Committee Changes Guarantee Method; Approves Several Loans 100

The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee held its tenth meeting at the China National Goods Bank on Tianjin Road on the 6th. The committee members present were Cai Zengji, Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoyan, Song Ziliang (representing Qin Runqing), Zhang Peishen, Xi Demao (representing Zhang Peishen), Chen Guangfu (representing Yu Zuoting), etc. Chairman Cai Zengji, in addition to reporting on routine committee affairs, also proposed 35 applications for small credit loans, which were reviewed one by one. It was resolved to grant loans at the original requested amount to six companies, to grant loans at half the requested amount to eleven companies, to grant loans at a reduced amount to fourteen companies, and to reject four companies. The reasons for rejection were as follows: (1) the factory has stopped and there is little hope for the future; (2) the capital was falsely reported, and the guarantor denied the guarantee; (3) the business has been losing money, and the guarantee is inadequate. Excluding those that were reduced or rejected, the committee actually approved loans totaling 21,400 yuan. It is said that the committee will send out notices within one or two days, instructing the applicants to go to the committee to sign the documents and collect the funds. Those who were rejected will also be notified, and the applicants can take back the previously issued receipt to collect the previously paid investigation fee of 2 yuan.

Flexible Guarantee

The Loan Committee recently submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to relax the requirement that loan guarantees should be sought from two reputable businesses, changing it to one business. In addition, for small loans of 100 yuan or less, the committee can stamp a certificate from the same industry association, with three businesses in the same industry providing a joint and several guarantee. These two cases are now in effect. Yesterday, the committee sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, informing the various industry associations that the problem of finding guarantees, which was the most difficult for industry and commerce, now has a flexible solution, and applying for loans should be more convenient than before.

Letter to the Chamber of Commerce

To Whom It May Concern:

This is to inform you that we have received Instruction No. 17685 from the Ministry of Finance, along with four documents submitted by this committee, to comply with the order to amend Articles 2(2) and 4(2) of the loan regulations and to request that the requirement for loan guarantees to be sought from reputable businesses be relaxed from two to one, and that small loans be allowed to be guaranteed by three businesses in the same industry with joint and several liability. We request your prompt review and approval to facilitate implementation. The directive stated: "We have received and examined all the submitted documents. After reviewing the proposed amendments to the loan regulations, it is believed that they are for the sake of military affairs and to protect industry and commerce. Approval should be granted to amend them separately. Apart from Article 2(2), which should be handled according to the wording of the original amendment, Article 4(2) should be amended to "(2) Small industrial and commercial credit loans should have a reputable business as a guarantor responsible for repayment (if it is a limited liability company, the manager of the company should be responsible for the guarantee). The assets of the borrower and the guarantor should be investigated and confirmed to be reputable. However, for small loans of 100 yuan or less, three businesses in the same industry may be allowed to provide joint and several guarantees, and the industry association must stamp a certificate." Please comply with these instructions and report back for our records. This order." In view of the above, regarding the section on allowing three businesses in the same industry to provide joint and several guarantees for small loans, we previously consulted with your chamber and have submitted reports separately, replied to you, and made separate recommendations to the Ministry to change the two business guarantees for loans to one business, in order to be considerate of industry and commerce and to provide practical relief. We now inform you of the above for your information and request that you inform the various industry associations accordingly. To the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Chairman Cai Zengji of the Committee.

The Eurasia Giant Plane: Expected to Arrive at Longhua Airport This Afternoon; General Characteristics of the Aircraft; Brief History of the Flight Crew 102

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation's Junkers JU52 giant plane, ordered from Germany, is scheduled to arrive at Shanghai's Longhua Airport at 3:00 PM today, flying from Guangzhou. The company has sent invitations to various sectors to attend the viewing. After arrival, the aircraft will be added to the newly opened Shaanxi-Chengdu air route. The aircraft is characterized as a perfect giant passenger plane, equipped with three engines. Its speed is extremely fast, and its ability to ascend and descend is also very agile. The cabin contains fourteen comfortable passenger seats, with a cargo hold at the rear of the fuselage. It is also equipped with washrooms, coat racks, luggage racks, and so on, possessing all kinds of new-style travel equipment. It is truly a most perfect passenger plane. The plane is flown to China by renowned German aviator Mr. Ludd. A brief history of him is introduced below: Mr. Ludd learned to fly in South Africa. During the European War, he fought against the British in Africa. In 1915, he was captured by the British. In 1916, after escaping back to Germany, he served in the German Air Force. In 1918, he fought against the Russian army. In Litau, he bailed out seven great generals, Enter Pasha and Talaat Pascha, from prison. Later, he served as a civil aviation pilot in Germany. In 1920, he worked in South America. In 1922, he worked for the German-Russian Aviation Corporation, and later for the German Hansa Aviation Corporation. He has flown over the highest mountain, the Alpen, 300 times. By February 27th of this year, he had flown one million kilometers, making him a pilot of extreme experience.

Chairman's Report

The association convened its second standing committee on August 3rd, presented it for discussion, and resolved on the spot to schedule a second general meeting of initiators to resolve the matter, and telegraphed the significance of the association's initiation of the hall construction and the progress of the situation to Chiang Kai-shek for review. The approval has not been received for a long time, resulting in the de facto suspension of all association affairs for a month and a half. Regarding financial matters, as of August 31st, after expenses, there was still a balance of one thousand eight hundred and ninety yuan, seven jiao, and one fen. The association received an order from Mayor Wu yesterday, relaying Chiang Kai-shek's order, which read, "Shanghai Mayor Wu, please translate and convey to Mr. Gu Xin-yi, Mr. Guo Shun, and Mr. Wu Zi-yuan: The matter of building the hall must not be carried out again to avoid serious offenses. Chiang Kai-shek, August 4th." After discussion, the following resolutions were made: (1) Respect Chiang Kai-shek's wishes and handle the conclusion; (2) Send another telegram to Chiang Kai-shek in the name of the general assembly to report on the initiation process; (3) First consult with each donor by letter to seek their consent to transfer the remaining funds to water disaster relief. As for the date of conclusion, it will be decided after another convening of the preparatory committee.

Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction Abolishes Silkworm Cocoon Monopoly; Manufacturers Allowed to Register Purchases; Zhejiang Silk Factory Requests Abolition of Improvement Fee 105

As the purchase of autumn cocoons is imminent, silk manufacturers in Zhejiang Province have jointly submitted a request to the Executive Yuan's Ministries of Finance and Industry, clearly ordering the abolition of the improvement fee. The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction has abolished the silkworm cocoon monopoly in order to maintain the merchants' difficulties. The Real Industry News reporter has recorded the following details:

Submitting a Request to the Executive Yuan and Ministries to Abolish the Improvement Fee

The silk manufacturers in Zhejiang Province, due to the burden of the improvement fee levied by the Department of Construction, have specially sent Chen Jing-xian, Xu Xing-bin, and others to Shanghai to contact British merchants, and have submitted separate requests to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry, requesting the abolition of the improvement fee. The document reads, "Submitted regarding the levy of the fresh silkworm cocoon improvement fee, which lacks a legal basis. We earnestly request that you promptly correct it in order to relieve farmers and merchants and comply with the rule of law. Since the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction's Silkworm Monopoly Committee forcibly levied the improvement fee, silk cocoon merchants have jointly appealed repeatedly. The government clearly knows that it is illegal, and your Executive Yuan and ministries have repeatedly consulted Zhejiang to promptly correct the matter. It can be seen that justice resides in the hearts of the people, and government orders cannot be borrowed. However, the Zhejiang Silkworm Monopoly Committee, citing the slogan 'take it from the silkworms, use it for the silkworms,' levies repeatedly, disregarding everything. According to the cost of fresh cocoons, the levy is more than one-tenth, which is more burdensome than any other tax. Can we bear to ignore the people's appeals and disregard their suffering? However, the Department of Construction, under the control of the National Government, brazenly acts its own way. If the people are not worth pitying, what about the government's credibility? Now that the autumn cocoon harvest is about to begin again, this illegal and exorbitant levy, the improvement fee of one yuan and eight jiao per dan of fresh cocoons, is still being levied openly after the Executive Yuan's order to promptly correct it. How can we talk about the rule of law and relieving farmers and merchants? The manufacturers and others, after years of bankruptcy, are barely managing, already hanging by a thread. How can they endure further exorbitant levies? Therefore, we are compelled to jointly submit this request to your Executive Yuan and ministries for review and approval, promptly investigating and implementing Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Supervision of Local Finances, promulgated and revised by the Central Government in December of the 21st year of the Republic of China, clearly ordering the abolition of this unfounded fresh silkworm improvement fee in order to relieve farmers and merchants and comply with the rule of law. This would be a great benefit." Furthermore, a written statement was submitted, jointly signed by Xu Xing-bin, Chen Xiao-yun, and Chen Jing-xian, stating that Xu Xing-bin represented the Zhejiang Chang'an Silk Factory, Chu Han-bang represented the Xiu Lun Silk Factory, Zhu Wen-gao represented the Minsheng Silk Factory, Zhang You-yi and Chen Xiao-yun represented the Tiancheng Silk Factory, Chen Jing-xian represented the Fuxing Silk Factory, Wang Qi-qi represented the Tiaoxi Silk Factory, Jin Xiu-huang represented the Xianglun Silk Factory, Yu Jin-jiang represented the Chongyu Silk Factory, and Gu Li-sheng represented the Housheng Silk Factory.

Zhejiang Department of Construction Abolishes Monopoly

Since the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction implemented a monopoly on all silk in Zhejiang last year, it borrowed 1.8 million yuan from Shanghai banking groups this spring to purchase spring cocoons from zones 1 to 6, while zones 7 to 10 were allocated to manufacturers for purchase. This method was quite effective. Zhejiang silk cocoon merchants, due to the decline in overseas silk sales and the poor business of silk factories, were greatly affected by the monopoly. The Zhejiang Provincial Cocoon Industry Association Joint Office in Shanghai telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministries of Finance and Industry, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government this spring, requesting the abolition of the monopoly by district. The Executive Yuan consulted the Zhejiang Provincial Government for cancellation. At that time, the procedures of the provincial government had already been decided and could not be cancelled immediately, so it only agreed to purchase by district. Now it is learned that the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction, in order to consider the difficulties of merchants and support the development of the silk industry, has abolished the silkworm cocoon monopoly. Hereafter, manufacturers are allowed to register and purchase within the ten zones. Members of the Yanshan Cocoon Industry have reported to the Shanghai office that the registration for purchasing autumn cocoons [unclear] stopped at 5:00 PM yesterday. Manufacturers [unclear] in Shanghai are planning to go to Zhejiang within days to begin purchasing cocoons in the areas they have registered for.

No Need to Supplement Stamp Duty on Old Account Books; Clear Instructions from the Ministry of Finance 106

The new Stamp Tax Enforcement Law stipulates that for account books established before September 1st, if stamp duty has already been paid according to the old regulations, it is not necessary to add stamps according to the new law after September 1st, even if they continue to be used. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly interpreted and responded to this. In order to prevent misunderstandings by inspectors, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance again, requesting that it explain this to various provinces inside and outside the capital. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance issued Approval No. 6985 of the Tax Department, stating, "Your telegraphic inquiry is understood. Checking vouchers for withdrawing money, goods, and materials, as well as account books used for various trades, the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Duty stipulate that each book must be stamped with one jiao of stamp duty per year. Therefore, the validity of the stamp duty paid should end on the date of the annual commercial closing. If the closing is based on the fiscal year, it should end at the end of the fiscal year. This has been the practice in the past. Although the current Stamp Tax Law has been implemented, for this year's account books that were started before its implementation and have already been stamped with one jiao of stamp duty as required, their stamp duty validity has not yet expired and there is no need to supplement stamps according to the Stamp Tax Law. To avoid misunderstandings during enforcement and inspection, a clear explanation should be given. In addition to issuing separate consultations, you should be informed of this approval."

Zhuo Xian-shu Left for Italy Yesterday to Study; Expected to Return to China in Three Years 112

Mr. Zhuo Xian-shu, a native of Shantou, Guangdong, is 28 years old this year. He has recently been selected by the General Staff Headquarters of the Military Commission to study at the Army University in Italy. He departed yesterday (the 7th) on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso. More than 100 people went to the pier to see him off, including Central Committee member Zhang Zhen and friends Zhuo Xiao-liang, Tan Li-men, Li Ze-xiang, and Dong Wen-zhong. It is learned that Mr. Zhuo graduated from the 4th Infantry Division of the Whampoa Military Academy. He made significant contributions during the Northern Expedition. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, in order to further his studies, Mr. Zhuo was sent by the central government to Japan to study at the Army Infantry and Management School. He returned to China in 1933 and served as an instructor at the Central Military Academy. He is the author of "Theory and Practice of Wartime Homeland Air Defense" and "Research on Army Mobilization Mechanisms," and he co-translated "Essential Companion for Manchurian-Mongolian Operations" with classmate Shen Xiang-kui. All are well-known works in domestic military science. It is heard that Mr. Zhuo is expected to graduate and return to China in three years. At that time, he will make a great contribution to military science in China.

The Fourth Ship of the Dutch Liner Asia-Africa Line, the "Lotzwol", Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning; Docked at the Ruirong Factory Pier, Welcoming Visitors; Will Return to Africa on the First of Next Month After Dock Inspection 116

The fourth giant ship of the newly opened Asia-Africa ocean line by the Dutch Royal Rotterdam Lloyd, the "Lotzwol", arrived in Shanghai at 7 AM yesterday morning. It docked at the Yangshupu Ruirong Factory Pier, welcoming visitors to freely tour the ship. The ship is scheduled to depart for Africa on the first of next month. The following is an investigation and record of the details by a Real Industry News reporter.

Arrival Situation

The Dutch company's fourth giant ship, the Lotzwol, departed from Hong Kong on June 29. The maiden voyage sailed to Bangkok, Singapore, Batavia, Lodeleik, Meritiesti, Lichyulin, Damatielwei, Bobong, London, Boqin, Shanseske, Mombasa, Mashi, and then back through Singapore and Hong Kong to Shanghai. The ship arrived in port at approximately 6 AM yesterday morning and docked at the Ruirong Factory Pier at 7 AM, a 70-day voyage, making it the longest route among current mail ships. This eastbound voyage to Shanghai, both first-class and standard-class cabins, were fully booked and carried a large number of famous goods from Africa and other places.

Structure and Equipment

The structure and equipment of the ship are the same as the first ship, the Hademan. The ship is over 383 feet long, with a gross tonnage of 4,741 tons and a net tonnage of 2,945 tons. The speed is 14.5 nautical miles per hour. The ship has a total power of over 3,000 horsepower, with six layers of platform armor, first-class cabins with 43 beds, second-class cabins with 47 beds, and third-class cabins with 350 beds. There are five cargo holds. The first and second-class cabins are equipped with large dining rooms, smoking rooms, bathrooms, barbershops, etc. The decorations are very luxurious. The safety equipment includes six lifeboats, a radio station, and a nurse, making it extremely complete.

Dock Inspection

According to Captain Hector, the ship is visiting Shanghai for the first time. After unloading the cargo, it will be docked to inspect all the ship's machinery. It is scheduled to depart for Africa on the first of next month, and the Java Company staff will invite people from all walks of life to visit freely from today. The fifth ship, the "Tasman", is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the fourth of next month, and the sixth ship, the "Minderou", is also scheduled to arrive on the eighth of November.
