Bizarre Case of Husband and Concubine Found Dead in Tapu Fang, Rue Pére Robert, French Concession. Frequent Quarrels Between Wife and Concubine. Police Investigation Suggests Suicide, But Traces of a Violent Standoff Cannot Be Dismissed 119

In a single three-story building at No. 8, Tapu Fang, Rue Pére Robert, French Concession, Jiang Jinmei, a second landlord from Nanhui, and his concubine, Wang A’mei, a woman from Zhoupu, were found dead in their bedroom. The discovery was made around 7 AM yesterday morning. Both had their heads nearly severed, connected only by a sliver of skin at the neck, a truly gruesome sight. Most strangely, those living in the same house heard nothing during the night when the deaths occurred. Whether it was murder or suicide is yet to be determined by the police. In any case, the circumstances are bizarre and sudden. Detailed information is provided below:

Divorce and Remarriage

Jiang Jinmei was a native of Nanhui County, Pudong, currently 37 years old. He specialized in contracting bean curd residue in Shanghai, then selling it to villagers to feed pigs. He was initially married to a Hu woman from the same village, with whom he had a daughter named Xiuzhen, now fifteen years old. Due to disagreements, they divorced by mutual consent in 1932. Later, Jiang remarried to a young Li woman from Songjiang. After three years, Li had no children, so they adopted a son named Genlin, only three years old.

Taking a Concubine

Two years ago, Jiang rented a single three-story house at No. 8, Tapu Fang, near Tapu Bridge on Rue Pére Robert, French Concession. Besides Jiang, Li, Jiang's parents, Jiang Xianhai and Jiang Chu’shi, and his children, other tenants lived there. Last year, Jiang became romantically involved with Wang A’mei (18 years old this year), the daughter of Wang Ding’shi, a fellow tenant from Zhoupu. In mid-February of this year, Jiang formally took A’mei as his concubine. The two of them used the front room on the second floor as their bedroom.

Discord Between Wife and Concubine

The remarried Li led her children to live in the back parlor downstairs as their bedroom. Jiang's parents hired six or seven rickshaw pullers, who temporarily lived in the front parlor, working early and sleeping late, as was their custom. Jiang treated his wife and concubine equally on the surface, but he actually favored A’mei. As a result, the relationship between the wife and concubine deteriorated, and quarrels occurred frequently. Although Jiang tried to smooth things over, Li remained resentful. A’mei’s mother, Wang Ding’shi, moved out in April and resided at No. 24, Wu’an Fang, Rihui Road, Rihui Port, in the Chinese area because she felt uneasy after her daughter married Jiang.

Not Seen Descending

Since marrying Jiang, A’mei became pregnant and was eight months along, with her due date approaching. The day before yesterday (the 6th), around 6 PM, another argument broke out between the wife and concubine, but it stopped quickly. Around 7 PM, Jiang and A’mei went upstairs to sleep. Jiang's parents, Li, and children, along with other friends in the parlor, played mahjong until 9 PM, then went to bed. Around 7 AM yesterday morning, the people downstairs had been up for a while but hadn’t seen Jiang and A’mei come downstairs. Li ordered her daughter Xiuzhen to go upstairs and call them.

Covered in Bloodstains

Xiuzhen called repeatedly but received no response. Then, she knocked on the door, but there was still no sound. She asked Zhu Jiang’shi, a neighbor and fellow villager living in the second-floor pavilion, to call them. After a long time, there was still no reply, which aroused suspicion. Xiuzhen pushed the door forcefully, but it was locked with a spring lock, making it impossible to open from the outside. She quickly grabbed a ladder, climbed onto the partition wall, looked through the bullseye window, and saw the bed curtains and floor covered in bloodstains, with a foul smell. Greatly alarmed, she reported to Jiang's mother, Chu’shi, who then notified the Lou Jia Wan Central Police Station.

Headed Couple

The police, led by Western Inspector Folongdeng, Chief Inspector Pei’erqi, Chinese Inspector Jin Jiulin, Detectives Zhang Ziying and Zhou Buguang, rushed to kick open the door. Inside, they found Jiang and Wang completely naked, lying on the bed. Their necks had been cut about two-thirds through with a knife. Contrary to rumors, their abdomens were not cut open. Jiang Jinmei was found face down on the floor near the window, with one foot in a foot bath bucket. Next to the bucket was a sharp knife about a foot long and two inches wide, the suspected murder weapon. Jiang’s neck had been cut one-third through. He was shirtless, barefoot, and wearing white cotton shorts. Both bodies were covered in bloodstains. The bed, mosquito net, and floor were also stained with blood. The detectives questioned the residents living upstairs and downstairs, who all claimed that it was quiet all night, which was very strange.

Court Examination

Later, the police found several suicide notes from the deceased Jiang Jinmei in the drawer of the dressing table, stating the reasons for his suicide. However, family members said that the deceased could not write. After detailed examination by Chinese and Western detectives, the family members living in the house were taken to the police station for questioning. Detective Wu Wengang was assigned to guard the deceased's home. Detective Zhang Chunsheng notified the Tongren Auxiliary Hall, ordering an undertaker to transport the bodies to the coroner's office. The Second Special Court was notified, and Judge Wang Ren and Chief Forensic Doctor Peng Hu arrived at the scene at 3:30 PM to conduct a detailed autopsy.

Resembling Suicide

According to the report of Detective Zhang Chunsheng, the police believed that Jiang Jinmei first killed his concubine and then committed suicide. The judge questioned the deceased’s parents, wife, and daughter, Jiang Xianhai, Jiang Chu’shi, Jiang Li’shi, and Jiang Xiuzhen, as well as witness Zhu Jiang’shi, who all testified that they did not hear any noise during the night and did not know how the deaths occurred. Jiang Xianhai requested that the bodies be collected for burial. The judge ruled that Jiang Jinmei and Jiang Wang’shi died from knife wounds and that the bodies were to be claimed by Jiang Xianhai for burial.

Hints and Clues

It was also said that after Jiang took Wang as his concubine, Jiang’s wife, Li, felt neglected and became restless. She had an affair with a gangster named "Lala’tou A’wu," whom she called "old man." Jiang discovered the location and time of their rendezvous and went with an axe to catch them in the act, injuring the lover with three axe blows. Friends intervened and mediated. Soon after, Wang discovered the place where Li was having an affair. Wang went there to catch them in the act. The lover, alert, heard the noise, jumped out of the window, and hired someone to extort 260 yuan from Wang. Because of this, the wife and concubine had a deep grudge. Now, the sudden deaths of Jiang and his concubine raised suspicion. The French police are currently investigating.

About to Perform the Dotting Ceremony, Suddenly Stopped, Snatching Away the Ancestral Tablet. Younger Brother Unwilling to Let Elder Brother Decide Funeral Alone, Elder Brother Reports to Police, Sent to Court for Trial 120

Fei Keming of this county, a landowner by profession, possessing 200,000-300,000 yuan, had four sons and two daughters: eldest son Fei Yusheng, second son Junwen, third son Bingwen, and youngest son Meiwen. Daughters were named Guijin and Meijin. Except for Yusheng and Meiwen, who lived separately at No. 4, North Sichuan Road, the rest lived with their father at No. 70, Lane 741, Dongyouheng Road. Fei Keming, 65, passed away on August 4th due to illness. The funeral arrangements were entirely managed by the eldest son, Yusheng. The dotting ceremony was scheduled for the day before yesterday, the leading ceremony yesterday, and the funeral at 3 PM. The person invited to perform the dotting ceremony was a Mr. Xu, a teacher at a certain law school, and also Junwen's teacher. At 3:30 PM the day before yesterday, just before the dotting ceremony, Fei Junwen brought a self-defense pistol to stop it, snatching away the ancestral tablet and declaring that the funeral would not be allowed. Fei Yusheng asked him to return the ancestral tablet but was refused, causing the dotting ceremony to be canceled. Fei Yusheng reported to the Huishan Police Station. Detectives Huang Fugen and Wang Tongpo investigated and charged Fei Junwen with the crime of desecrating funeral and sacrificial rites. They obtained an arrest warrant from the First Special District Court and arrested Fei Junwen at 10 PM the night before yesterday. Along with a self-defense pistol and 70 bullets, he was taken to the police station for detention and sent to the Fifth Criminal Division of the First Special Court yesterday morning. Judge Huang Risheng questioned him. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated the case, prosecuting him under Article 146, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, and claiming that the accused had refused to reveal where he hid the ancestral tablet, indicating that he still intended to obstruct the funeral. Therefore, bail should not be granted. Although the accused had a license for the pistol, it expired in January. The police would handle it separately. Fei Yusheng testified that he specially invited his teacher to conduct the dotting ceremony for fear that the accused would object to the dotting ceremony, but the accused still interfered. He recounted the situation at the time. Fei Junwen argued that the father’s funeral should have been discussed by all the brothers and sisters, but the plaintiff acted unilaterally without consulting them. He did not even know who was invited to perform the dotting ceremony. Moreover, the ancestral tablet was taken by his sister and then given to him, not snatched. The plaintiff did not specify anything in the obituary today. His lawyer, Jiang Guofang, stated that the case was entirely due to family property disputes. After Fei Keming's death, the plaintiff, along with the youngest brother, took away all the iron boxes, deeds, and silver dollars. The funeral was entirely managed by him without consulting the defendant. In old customs, the dotting ceremony was extremely important. The person performing the ceremony must be prestigious, blessed with five fortunes, and their birth date must not conflict with the deceased, as this affected the prosperity of future generations. The plaintiff acted unilaterally, which was inappropriate. The police's request to deny bail was inappropriate, because if the funeral was indeed held today, the defendant's rights as a filial son should be protected. He requested that the defendant be allowed to leave. Judge Huang reviewed the testimony and ordered the case to be adjourned to next Wednesday for further questioning. The defendant was granted a 500-yuan bond and allowed to be released, with strict orders not to obstruct the funeral, or he would be severely punished. Fei Junwen agreed and left the court.

The Great Fish Market Scheduled to Open in Early October, Magnificent Architecture, Precision Design, Final Stages of Construction Currently Underway 122

According to Shen Shi News Agency, the Ministry of Industry has raised over one million yuan to build a large-scale fish market in Yangshupu, Shanghai, to revitalize our fishing industry. The internal construction is nearing completion and is scheduled to open in early October. The market building is very magnificent, and the design is highly precise, making it our country's only great fish market. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency has detailed the internal construction as follows:

Scheduled Opening

The market is located about five li north of Dinghai Bridge in Yangshupu, at Zhoujiazuidao, facing the Huangpu River and across from Shanghai University. It faces the Huangpu River and backs the Dinghai River, with the Qiujiang Pier, which is under construction, to the north. Covering an area of over forty mu, it is not only large in scale but also conveniently located for transportation. The construction is expected to be completed this month and is scheduled to open in early October.

Overview of the Project

The completed structures include brokers' offices, auction yards, offices, a weather station, and riverside warehouses. The construction was undertaken by the Xinchangtai Construction Company. The brokers' offices are three stories high, with about eighty rooms. The auction yard is in front of the brokers' offices, shaped like a ring. The market office building is seven stories high. The accounting and bank office and a storage room are on the left side of the ground floor. The second floor has a reception room, the general affairs office, etc. The third floor has eight rooms, all for staff dormitories. The fourth, fifth, and sixth floors each have one room, also for staff dormitories. The seventh floor is the weather station. The riverside warehouses have also been completed.

Active Construction

The floating dock project includes three steel docks. The Shanghai Pudong Shipyard is constructing a shipyard for 80,000 yuan. The longest dock was launched on June 1st. The pile driving has been completed, and they are now driving platform piles. The Bund Dredging Bureau has dredged the area around the Pujiang Marsh Dock with a dredger. Once the platform is completed, the floating dock can be installed. The cold storage is being built by the American York Company of Shanghai for over 270,000 yuan, starting on April 10th. It is divided into four parts: cold storage, ice making, freezing, and machinery. The installation of machinery could have started earlier, but the cold storage room structure was remodeled, and the soil was alluvial. The Bund Dredging Bureau conducted an inspection, which delayed the work. Currently, the ice-making machinery has started to be installed and is expected to be completed this month. Additionally, the artesian well water tower has been completed. In the near future, this national state-run great fish market will be completed.

Suddenly Disappeared

The next day, Fan Asan's body was found in a desolate place on Ma Yushan Road, with knife wounds on her neck, clearly indicating that she had been murdered. After the court accepted the case and conducted an investigation, due to the lack of corroborating evidence, Pei Xueshi was not prosecuted. Zeng Fan's refused to accept this and appealed to the High Court for reconsideration. As a result, the basis for the appeal was deemed insufficient, and he was still not prosecuted. Zeng Fan's still refused to accept this and filed a third appeal for reconsideration. Zhang Zi, the prosecutor, tirelessly sought details, repeatedly summoned witnesses, and conducted a thorough investigation, concluding that Pei Xueshi had strong suspicion of instigating murder.

Major Suspicion

He filed a lawsuit with the criminal court, requesting a public trial for Pei Xueshi, who was ordered to find a suitable guarantor to await instructions. The main points of the indictment were roughly as follows: The defendant, Pei Xueshi, cohabitated with the concubine of the late Zheng Kaijun in November of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. He gradually squandered more than 1,000 yuan in foreign currency that Fan Asan had privately saved. On July 16th of the previous year, due to an incident, he quarreled and injured Fan Asan's head. After mediation, Pei Xueshi gave a promissory note for 500 yuan, which led to resentment. Pei Xueshi, fearing future trouble because Fan Asan had hidden the promissory note in her sister Hui Fan's house,

Intended to Murder

On January 6th of this year, at 6:00 PM, he incited an unidentified man to go to 255 Yangzhou Road to invite Fan Asan out on the pretext of negotiating a price. He designed to lure her into a car and drive to a desolate place on Ma Yushan Road, where he killed her with a knife. After the incident, Zeng Fan's filed a lawsuit. The examination of the deceased Fan Asan revealed a cut at the right corner of her lower lip, connecting to her right jaw, a cut in her throat, and her trachea was severed. Her left ring finger had been cut off, indicating that she died from her injuries. After opening the coffin, Zeng Fan's and Pei Xueshi confirmed that it was indeed her. The unidentified man invited Fan Asan out on that day, which was also confirmed by Dong Shaoyuan, Fan Asan's landlord at 255 Yangzhou Road, who testified to Pei Xueshi's

Hostile Relationship

Not only did Zeng Fan's state this, but Fan Asan had also previously filed a case against Pei for assault. Fan Asan did not hide the 500 yuan promissory note given to her by Pei Asan in her own house but instead hid it in her sister Zeng Fan's house. From this, it can be seen that their feelings were broken and they were irreconcilable. If the unidentified man was not Pei's friend, why would Fan Asan rashly go with him to Ma Yushan Road? Before the incident, a car was discovered parked at the scene of the incident. Although this was a one-sided statement from Zeng Fan's, it coincided with the time Fan Asan left, and it was credible. In conclusion, Pei Xueshi had strong suspicion of instigating the murder of Fan Asan, and he committed the crime under Article 371, paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, etc. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Judge Tan Zhuohong specially opened the Eleventh Tribunal to interrogate the defendant Pei Xueshi. Lawyers Yan Shenshi, Wu Kaisheng, Zhu Honglie, and others appeared in court to defend him. The plaintiff, Zeng Fan's, hired lawyer Su Fuchou to appear in court and request a private prosecution for over 3,000 yuan. First, witness

Ding Buying testified

Age 29, formerly a peddler, residing at Gaolang Bridge. In February of this year, I don't remember the date, I went to Zeng Fan's house to chat. At that time, Pei Xueshi was also in Fan's house. I heard Pei Xueshi say to Zeng Fan's, "Don't sue me. I am willing to find Asan's body and perform rituals for her," etc. I don't know anything else. Next, the defendant's mother, Pei Zhu's, and the defendant's wife, Xiao Pei Zhu's, were called to court. According to

Old Pei Zhu's

Age 50, from Yancheng, residing at 34 Changan Road, Zhabei. Xiao Pei Zhu's, age 32, lives with her mother-in-law. The official asked if they had gone to take things from Fan Asan's house. Pei Zhu's and others replied that they had not taken anything. The official said, "How can you say you didn't take anything when the landlord witnessed it?" They replied that they didn't know. The official ordered Pei Xueshi to the dock, age 33, from Yancheng. He asked if he had gone to Zeng Fan's house and said that he was willing to find Asan's body and invite monks to perform rituals. He replied that he had never been there. Zeng Fan's and Ding Buying are relatives, and they colluded to frame me. I am actually very wronged. The official said that the testimonies of the witnesses were very inconsistent. The case is serious, and the witnesses probably did not dare to testify casually. The official, for the sake of caution, ordered Zeng Fan's to leave the court.

Separate Interrogation

He then asked Ding Buying what exactly happened. The case concerns human life, and he should testify truthfully without being vague. He replied that Pei Xueshi was sitting on a stool, and I was sitting on the bed next to him. Zeng Fan's was cooking at around 2:00 PM. The official obtained his testimony and ordered Zeng Fan's to the dock, then questioned her in detail. Her testimony was largely the same as above. When questioned by Pei Xueshi, he vehemently claimed injustice, firmly stating that they were relatives and had colluded to frame him, and requested an investigation. The official considered the circumstances of the case to be complicated and did not open the debate today, but scheduled a continuation of the hearing after a detailed investigation. The defendant Pei Xueshi was ordered to be detained pending further instructions. The defendant's lawyer then requested that he still be released on the original bond. The defendant argued that he was a constable in the patrol room, and imprisonment would hinder his duties. The official considered the case to be serious and did not approve it. Finally, the court clerk ordered him to be taken into custody.

Zhang Chunshan, the owner of a shoe store at 272 North Sichuan Road, whose daughter's name is Yu Bao, (age 18) is petite and charming. Wanyi Sha Factory Oiling Worker Wan Wenkui Breaks Right Hand and Dies 136

The New Yu Second Yarn Factory at No. 8 Labosheng Road was formerly the Puyi Yarn Factory. It was taken over by a new owner on February 20th of this year and changed its name to the current name. It was unexpected that yesterday morning at 2:00 AM, an oiling worker named Wan Wenkui, (from Yancheng, age 30) was working in the weaving workshop when he suddenly saw a leather belt on a stocking break. He climbed up the ladder to repair it, but at that time the machine was still running, causing him to be careless for a moment and his right hand was caught in the machine. He was unable to break free. His colleagues Liu Zhaoqing and others caught sight of it and quickly stopped the machine, but Wan's right wrist had already been severed and separated from his body, and his legs were also severely injured. He fell from a height of fifteen feet. Afterwards, the factory reported it to the Putuo Road Police Station in charge, and Detective Pi Shaozhang and others were dispatched to investigate. They summoned an ambulance to send Wan and his severed hand to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He soon died. His body was transported to the Ferren Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Song Genshan, an inspector from the First Special District Court, together with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. According to witness Liu Zhaoqing's statement, and Wan's mother, Wan Zhou's, who claimed to be 53 years old, residing in a thatched shed at Zhujiawan, Zhabei, stated that the deceased was her eldest son and had worked at the factory for more than ten years. Now that he had died while working, there were still several elderly and young people in the family who depended on him for a living, and she requested generous compensation. According to Li Laobo, the personnel manager of the factory, the deceased died in the line of duty, and according to factory regulations, compensation of 150-160 yuan should be given, but seeing that his family was poor, they specially increased the compensation to 220 yuan and stated that they had already purchased coffins and other items. Mr. Song, noting that there was no severed hand of the deceased in the morgue, inquired with Chinese Detective Pi Shaozhang. He reported that after the deceased had an accident at the factory, he accompanied him to the hospital, and the severed hand was not missing. Later, when the hospital transported the body to the morgue, he was not present. He requested that the deceased's family accompany him to the hospital to inquire about the situation. Mr. Song approved it and instructed that the deceased Wan Wenkui, male, had indeed died from machine injuries before his death. The body was handed over to his mother, Wan Zhou's, who signed a bond to take it back for coffining and burial. He also instructed Luo Zhengchao, the manager of the factory's machinery, to be extra careful and improve the prevention of such unfortunate events in the future to avoid the recurrence of the same tragedy.

Shanghai Telegraph Bureau Strictly Prohibits Messengers from Demanding Liquor Money; Ministry of Communications Re-emphasizes by Telegram 140

The Ministry of Communications, considering that the Mid-Autumn Festival according to the lunar calendar will soon arrive, sent an urgent telegram to the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, which read, "It has been strictly forbidden for messengers to demand liquor money. As the Mid-Autumn Festival is approaching, it is inevitable that messengers from various bureaus and stations will still follow the old custom of demanding money from recipients or receiving festival rewards. Various bureaus and stations should assign personnel to conduct real-time inspections. If the above is found, it should be punished in accordance with the regulations." The bureau, in addition to notifying all affiliated messengers to comply, printed and distributed a notice and is conducting investigations outside at any time and sincerely requests all parties to report as much as possible so that a thorough investigation can be conducted and people can avoid being harassed.

Sports News

Preliminary Athletics Trials for the City's National Games: Dai Shuguo Sets National Record in 400 Meters—Time: 52 Seconds Even—Women's 100 Meters and Long Jump Results Are Promising—One Participant in the Decathlon Will Not Continue Today—Official Representatives Still Need to Be Selected by the Selection Committee 144

The autumn air is crisp and refreshing, the perfect time for athletes to show their skills. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the city's supplementary trials for athletes to attend the National Games in athletics were held at Jiaotong University. Although there were only fifty or sixty athletes participating, they were full of vigor. In the men's events, Dai Shuguo broke the national record in the 400 meters with a time of 52 seconds even (the national record was Liu Changchun's 52.4 seconds), which was the best achievement of the competition. In the women's events, Qian Hangsu's time of 13.5 seconds in the 100 meters was relatively outstanding.

Guests from Afar

It has already been decided who will represent the city in athletics at the National Games. This supplementary election is to ensure that no talent is overlooked and to give an opportunity to those who have not participated in the city's summer training camp. Among the special guests attending the competition yesterday were Lin Shaozhou, who previously represented Fujian, Dai Shuguo, and the Shandong girls Zhu Tianzhen and Ding Guimei. However, Miss Pang Yuanyu from Changshu, although she had registered, did not attend the competition.

Competition Situation

What was disappointing yesterday was that Zhang Jiaqi did not attend the long jump and triple jump, and was eliminated after only competing in the 100 meters. Dai Shuguo finished fourth in the 100-meter final, and then jumped to the top in the 400 meters, maintaining a consistent pace from start to finish. In the upcoming National Games, he will be a strong opponent for Dong Shuzhao. Also, Lin Shaozhou took to the field despite being ill. It is heard that he is suffering from a severe cough, so he did not dare to exert himself fully during the competition, resulting in mediocre results. Also, Dai Junchang's time in the 800 meters, 2 minutes and 8.6 seconds, was quite impressive. If he represents the city in the National Games in the future, he may have a chance of finishing fifth or sixth. The results of the men's events from the north are not worth mentioning.

Women's Athletics

In the women's athletics competition, Little Qian won first place in both the 50 meters and 100 meters, with the 100-meter result being better. There was no final in the 200 meters because no one participated. In the high jump, Zhu Tianzhen won first place with 1.29 meters. In the shot put, Ding Guimei won first place with a score of 9.14 meters, which may also win points for the city in the future. However, Shi Ouqing was helpless yesterday due to a foot injury. In the long jump, she was defeated by Chen Zaichun. Chen Zaichun won the long jump with 4.83 meters. It is a pity that Qian Hangsu gave up this event, and Miss Pang did not come, so Chen reigned supreme.

All-Around Competition

Yesterday, three people joined the pentathlon and only Wei Zhiping joined the decathlon. The results were mediocre. Wei Zhiping did not complete the first half and, because his results were too poor, it was decided that the second half would not be held today. Sun Huipeng won first place in the pentathlon with a score of 2057 points, which was calculated using the latest published scoring method of the National Games, which is slightly less advantageous than the old scoring method.

Snippets from the Venue

Dai Shuguo Lives Up to Expectations

The 400-meter expert Dai Shuguo came to Shanghai to serve this time. Yesterday, he tested his skills for the first time in the preliminary round, attracting many fans to watch. Dai planned to participate in three events: 100 meters, 200 meters, and 400 meters. He finished first in the preliminary round of the 100 meters with 11.8 seconds, but fell to fourth place in the final, which greatly disappointed the audience. However, the 100 meters is not Dai's forte, so he gave up participating in the 200 meters to conserve his energy. Sure enough, he showed his skills in the 400 meters, leading all the way to the finish line, breaking Liu Changchun's national record of 52.4 seconds with 52 seconds. The audience cheered again and again.

Lin Shaozhou Takes to the Field Despite Being Ill

Lin Shaozhou of Fujian, who holds the national record of 16.2 seconds in the 110-meter hurdles, was also the focus of attention. However, Lin completed the race in 17.5 seconds. Although he won the championship, his results regressed. According to Lin, he has had a cold for two weeks and has not recovered since coming to Shanghai. Recently, his cough has worsened. He took to the field despite being ill, and his footwork was not strong. Moreover, the northerly winds were very strong yesterday, and running against the wind also affected his results. After a few days of rest, he can still restore his previous record.

Pang Yuanyu's Fragrant Figure Is Gone

Miss Pang is from Changshu and has a long jump result that broke the provincial record in the Jiangsu Provincial Games. This semester, she came to Shanghai to study at Dongya (some say Aiguo) and also registered to participate in the city's preliminary round. The fans in Shanghai all wanted to see the style of the small group from Changshu, but unexpectedly, due to physiological reasons, she could not participate yesterday, so her fragrant figure was nowhere to be found in the venue.

Zhu Tianzhen's Results Decline

Miss Zhu Tianzhen from Shandong is a famous general who holds the national women's high jump record. She also participated yesterday. Due to a long period of disuse, her legs were stiff. She had to jump four times to clear 1.29 meters, which is far from her original record of 1.355 meters. The second place, Niu Zaichun, was 1.23 meters, and the third place, Yang Ying, was 1.20 meters.

Chen Zaichun Jumps Well

Chen Zaichun's long jump yesterday was 4.83 meters, which is equal to Li Senzhi's result and not far from the National Games record of 4.88 meters. With a little more practice, it will not be difficult to break it. Shi Ouqing originally stood out in the All-Nations Games. Yesterday, she suddenly injured her ankle when jumping to 4.35 meters and could not jump any further, finishing third. At the same time, she cancelled her scheduled participation in the 100 meters and high jump and left.

Qian Hangsu Runs Faster and Faster

Miss Qian Hangsu has already held the national records in the 200 meters, low hurdles, and long jump. Yesterday, she also participated in the 50 meters and 100 meters. Her 50-meter result was 7.4 seconds and her 100-meter result was 13.5 seconds, which are not far from the national records. It is possible that she will give up the long jump and switch to the 100 meters in the upcoming National Games.

10,000 Meters: Only Two Arrived

Fourteen people participated in the 10,000 meters. Veterans Wan Jinsheng and Zhou Ruquan both participated, but retired halfway due to exhaustion. Qian Zenglong originally had hopes of winning the championship, but his old illness relapsed in the fifteenth lap and he had to withdraw. Only Ling Xuewen and Bao Yibi completed the course.

City Swimming Pool to Open Today: Mayor to Cut Ribbon, Ms. Chen Baoxuan to Perform Inaugural Swim: International Competition Scheduled for the 12th, Public Competition for the 22nd 145

The city's municipal swimming pool is scheduled to officially open this afternoon (the 8th) at 2:00 PM. At that time, in addition to the mayor personally cutting the ribbon and performing the opening ceremony, Ms. Chen Baoxuan, a former swimming champion, will be invited to perform the inaugural swim. There will also be a practice performance by the city's athletes participating in the National Games. This afternoon, admission will be by invitation only. Admission tickets will be sold for two dimes per ticket, starting from 10:00 AM today in front of the swimming pool. Regarding the officials in charge of the opening ceremony, the municipal government has assigned the following: Li Dachao for reception, Lin Yannan, Xia Chuande, Chen Tianyou, Zhang Yinhuai, Chen Tongjia, Wang Keshui, Lu Hailan, Secretary Zhou Guoping, Li Shigen, Liu Xunru, Cheng Pengnian, Wu Yiqun, Da Zhongge, Zhang Zhuo, Gao Shengjiang Shicheng, Rescue Student Zhang Rongguang, Sun Junmeng, Master of Ceremonies Lin Yannan, Engineering Office Dong Daxi, Wang Huabin, Liu Zhong, Management Office Li Dachao, Yu Binqi, and it is heard that Mayor Wu has decided to hold an international swimming competition on the 12th of this month and a citywide public swimming competition on the 22nd.

Opening Ceremony: The order of the opening ceremony of the pool is as follows: (1) All stand at attention, (2) Play music, (3) Sing the party song, (4) Pay the most respectful tribute to the Party-State and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (5) Silence, (6) Mayor's speech, (7) Opening ceremony, (8) Performance competition, (9) Play music, (10) Completion.

Pool Construction: The pool is an open-air type, surrounded by a grandstand that can accommodate 5,000 people. Under the grandstand are dressing rooms, shower rooms, rest rooms, shops, public toilets, corridors, water delivery, etc. On the north side of the grandstand is a grand main entrance. Inside the entrance are offices, a reception room, a hall, ticket offices, etc. Corridors are built along the east, west, and south sides of the grandstand to meet the needs of spectators for shelter from the rain. Regarding the dimensions of the swimming pool, it conforms to the swimming competition regulations of American universities. The pool surface is 18 meters (60 feet) long and 6 meters (20 feet) wide. The depth of the pool is 9 centimeters (3 feet) at the shallow end and 1.5 meters (5 feet) at the deep end. The edges of the pool are spoon-shaped in the direction of the long side, starting from a depth of about 1 meter 1 cm (2 and a half feet) at the end and gradually deepening towards the center to a depth of 1 meter 7 cm (5 and a half feet). The distance from the center to the other end is 5 meters (16 feet), and the land falls by 3.5 meters (11 and a half feet) (this depth is used by the Far Eastern Games). The pool is constructed of reinforced concrete and waterproof materials, which are sufficient to resist the "water pressure" when the pool is full and the "earth pressure" when the pool is empty. 725 piles were driven into the bottom of the pool as a foundation. The bottom and sides of the pool are paved with white mosaic, and the four sides are lined with white ceramic tiles.

Performance Program: (1) Basic exercises, (2) 50-meter freestyle: Shan Jiewei, Zhang Rongguang, Huang Rixiong, Chen Yuquan, Chen Wenhe, Zhu Jiongpei, He Ridian, Lu Huijie, (3) Women's 50-meter freestyle: Liu Suxian, Chen Binyi, Wang Aixian, Jian Dingying, Li Guiling, Yang Yiying, (4) 100-meter breaststroke: Jian Erjie, Jian Erwei, Zhong Shoujun, Wu Gansheng, Women's 50-meter swimming: Zhou Xiuzhen, Ren Juanjuan, He Wenjin, Yang Shuying, Zhang Jiaqi, (6) 400-meter freestyle: Shi Jiangen, Zhang Shangqi, Lu Yikui, Zhang Huimin, (7) 50-meter backstroke: Zheng Zhongying, Yang Shuying, He Wenjin, Li Lingli, (8) Zigonmeter backstroke: Ci Erming, Xu Zhangqiang, Huang Zhili, Wu Lingzhong, Shen Jiarong, (9) 100-meter freestyle, Wei sheng, Huang Rixiong, Zhang Rongguang, He Ridian, Chen Wenhe, Zhu Jingjing, (10) Ninety-meter breaststroke, Six-year-old soldier Yang Qiying, (11) Women's 100-meter freestyle, Liu Suxi, Chen Shixuan, Zhu Aixian, (12) Game: Blind swimming, Pushing rickshaws, (13) Fancy relay First group Xu Shouqiang (back, ) Wu Gansheng (breast, ) Liang Weisheng (freestyle) Second group Huang Zhili (back, ) Jian Erjie (breast, ) Chen Baoquan, Third group Huang Rixiong (back, ) Jian Erming (breast, ) Zhang Rongguang (freestyle) (14) Lifesaving performance,

(1) Famous athletes and staff should assemble in the hall of the Pi Chuan Road Youth Association before 1:00 PM today and take the special vehicle provided by the city government together. Do not go there by yourself to avoid misunderstandings. (2) Because the diving board in the city's pool has not yet been installed properly, diving athletes cannot perform. Educational News

Ministry of Education Sets November 10th for Qualification Examination; Yesterday's Order to National Vocational Schools Above the Specialized Level: Students of Unregistered and Closed Private Vocational Schools Must Pay Attention! 159

(Nanjing, 7th dispatch) The Ministry of Education has set November 10th of this year for the qualification examination in Shanghai and Peiping. This was reported in this newspaper on the 4th of this month. Yesterday (the 7th), the Ministry of Education ordered all vocational schools above the specialized level across the country, stating: "This Ministry has held several qualification examinations for graduates and students of unregistered and closed private vocational schools above the specialized level, and has clearly indicated that such examinations will no longer be held. However, many students are still waiting and watching, and have not participated promptly, which is a missed opportunity. However, there are also those who have not been able to participate due to location or other reasons, which is understandable. In order to take into account the studies and qualifications of these students, it is decided to hold another qualification examination in Peiping and Shanghai on November 10th of this year as a form of relief. All public and registered private vocational schools above the specialized level must order students from unregistered and closed private vocational schools above the specialized level whose admission qualifications have not been approved by this Ministry in previous reports of new students to participate in this qualification examination and obtain transfer qualifications. All documents must be submitted by each school to the Ministry by February of the 25th year for verification. If the reports are not submitted by the deadline, the Ministry will cancel the students' academic status. In addition to issuing notices, this order is issued for compliance and to inform all students. Furthermore, when schools recruit new students and transfer students in the future, they should uniformly admit those who hold a transfer certificate issued by this Ministry. Graduates should also be allowed to take the entrance examination for the fourth year, and after passing the examination, they may be admitted to the final year of study without being restricted by Article 4 of the University Regulations and Article 4 of the Revised Vocational School Regulations. You are to comply with this order."

Shandong Province Implements Compulsory Education, Opening 3,000 Schools 160

(Jinan, 7th dispatch) Compulsory education throughout the province began in August, opening in three phases and twenty districts, with a total of 3,000 schools. Each school has 80 students, totaling 240,000 students per year. The annual cost is 785,000 yuan. In addition, compulsory education and ordinary primary school teachers will be used to give lectures on general knowledge to villagers, with 10,000 locations throughout the province, lecturing twice a week. 320,000 patriotic knowledge and health knowledge posters will be printed for temporary reference during lectures. Schools will also be set up in 300 severely disaster-stricken areas to provide education.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

How to Organize a Children's Science Research Association? 171

— Linghu Zhao

When you see the term "science," you must feel it is boring and tasteless. In fact, if you are a little patient and study it slowly, you will discover that "science" is a very interesting thing.

I know very well that teachers must have explained the importance of "science" to you more than once, right? However, teachers have never pointed out "science" to you and taught you how to learn it, have they?

When you enter the fifth and sixth grades, you will have new courses, such as nature, history, and society, which are actually "science"! As for arithmetic, it is a tool for studying "science." Do you understand?

Now I will write down the method of organizing a "Children's Science Research Association":

(1) It is best to form a group for each grade, and the fifth and sixth grades form two groups, forming a single association. The number of people should be at most 60, with ten people in each team.

(2) Each team has two team leaders, one chief and one deputy.

(3) Hold a team leader meeting once a week and a general meeting once a month.

(4) Membership fees are two small ocean dollars per person, used to purchase equipment and books.

(5) If there are any difficulties with any grass or tree, ask each other for advice. Finally, you can send representatives to ask the teachers, and you must not stop until you understand thoroughly.

(6) Which team reports in detail and correctly, and which team studies thoroughly, will be judged by the joint team leaders, and the best few teams will be purchased prizes to encourage them. Well, children, let's all get up and organize!

International Storms of Thunder and Lightning 172

— Kang Jianzhai Fu

The storms of war have already spread like thunder and lightning between Europe and Africa! Children, you have all seen and heard it, haven't you?

The Italian leader Mussolini had long regarded Abyssinia in East Africa as his own. Abyssinia was originally a semi-civilized black country in East Africa, a large piece of fat meat coveted by all white people that had not yet been disposed of. On the international stage, Abyssinia was an unknown soldier. How could he dare to fight against Italy, a first-class white power? He was naturally unwilling to submit, preferring to die rather than surrender. He longed for the powerful British and Americans to be his bodyguards. You see, before the war even started, he ceded the oil mining rights, which accounted for more than half of the country's total area, to the African Development Company of the British and American side. In order to cover up their peace proposals, the British and Americans had to temporarily give up their possession of these oil rights due to Italy's accusation. However, Italy still declared that it would act freely and not allow the League of Nations to stop it.

The British Empire has long been the hegemon of the sea. For Italy to send troops, it must pass through the vital passages of the Mediterranean Sea and the Red Sea: these passages are all under the control of the British Navy.

Now Italy's attitude towards Abyssinia is like a mantis catching a cicada. The cicada falls into the mantis's palm, but the mantis itself cannot but be wary of the oriole behind it—the British and Americans.

Although Britain ostensibly sings loudly about staying out of the situation and maintaining peace, it is actually consolidating its naval array in Malta and other places—vital passages in the Mediterranean—and does not allow it to be easily violated. Do you think Britain can avoid being drawn into the whirlpool if war breaks out? Once Britain declares mobilization, it will become a direct confrontation between Britain and Italy. Germany, France, the United States, Japan, and other countries all have intertwined interests, so the scope of the war will immediately expand. Isn't this the prelude to the Second World War?

Children! If a major war breaks out in the West, what will happen to us in East Asia? We must remember that less than twenty years ago, when the First World War was in progress, our neighbors took the opportunity to become active against us. You can ask your teachers about this story.

Now that the first major war is about to come again, how will the situation in East Asia change accordingly? Can we still hide in the cradle and have sweet dreams?

Matches 175

— Zhen

Playing with fire is something that Min'er often does. He often puts the black head of a match on the black surface of the matchbox. As long as he puts his thumb [blank space] on the black head and presses it slightly, the black head will burn. At the same time, he quickly releases it, so the black head falls down while burning. One day, he was playing like this again when his brother saw him.

"Min, you need to know that this thing is very dangerous. If you are not careful, you will burn your fingers. On the one hand, you are wasting a match for nothing, which is a pity."

"Brother, what's the pity in that? How much is a match worth? A box of matches is only one or two copper coins."

"Don't underestimate a match. Making a match requires many procedures and sweat,"

"How many procedures does it take to make a match?"

"In the old method of making matches, cotton had to be used for the wooden stick, which was even more time-consuming. So now the matchsticks are made of poplar branches. There are two types of matches: one is called the red-headed match, and the other is called the safety match. Red-headed matches are very dangerous because they are easy to burn, and the workers who make this kind of match are often poisoned because red-headed matches are made of yellow phosphorus. Yellow phosphorus is very poisonous, and eating 20% of it can kill people, so it is prohibited by the government authorities. Now what we see are all safety matches.

To make safety matches: 1. Dip one end of the matchstick into a flammable liquid, like candle oil for lighting. 2. Dip it into glue again, and when it dries, it becomes the match head. This glue is a mixture of sulfurized brother and gum. 3. The surface of the box is coated with red phosphorus, sulfurized ladder glass powder, and gum. This kind of match must be rubbed on a special box surface, otherwise it will not burn."

Butterfly 176

— Wen Yuyang

Butterflies are arthropods belonging to the insect class. There are many different kinds, approximately one hundred and forty-nine species. They have beautiful wings, a pair of club-shaped antennae on their heads, and a small abdomen covered with fine hairs. They do not have stinging barbs. During the day, they fly among flowers, sucking various flower juices. When at rest, their wings stand upright on their backs. Their pupae do not form cocoons, but instead use silk to hang from branches and walls. They are all a type of plant pest! Children, please look at the pictures on the left. For example, various swallowtail butterflies mostly harm fruit trees, and pierid butterflies mostly harm vegetables. Nymphalid butterflies, amathusiid butterflies, satyrid butterflies, lycaenid butterflies, hesperiid butterflies, mostly harm herbaceous plants and agricultural products. Think about it; they cause such harm to plants, which is very harmful to us. Indeed; even when you catch them to play with or make specimens, if you are not careful, they can damage your eyes. This is because their wings have very toxic powder. When you catch them, they struggle violently, and the toxic powder flies around. If it gets into your eyes, it can easily ruin our precious eyes!

(1-5) Swallowtail Butterfly Family (6-13) Nymphalid Butterfly Family (14) Amathusiid Butterfly Family (15-21) Pierid Butterfly Family (22-25) Lycaenid Butterfly Family (26-29) Satyrid Butterfly Family (30-33) Hesperiid Butterfly Family

Tiny Library 177

— Wang Shouqiu

Because I like to buy books, I have a lot of children's books at home. Recently, at Yun'er's request, I donated these children's books to her to start a small library, and I even bought her two bookshelves to display these books. So she joined forces with a dozen classmates and the neighbor's daughters to start it wholeheartedly.

The library is located in a small room. Inside, in addition to two bookshelves, there is a small table and a few small benches. Every day after school, they hide in that small room to read. If there is something they don't understand, or a word they don't know, they come and ask me. Although I find it a bit of a bother, their progress is very fast.

In addition to being open every day, they can also borrow books to read. They have a small booklet. The person borrowing the book writes the title and their name in this booklet, and then they can take it out! When they return it, they cross it out with a pen.

Normally, Yun'er and the others each have one dime for candy money every day. Now they save this money to buy books. Other children also often donate books to this small library, so their books are increasing day by day. Children! Does your dad have books? If so, you can do this too!

Animal Anecdotes 178

— Bing Yu

There are over forty types of deer in the world. Those produced in Northeastern China are called "Guandong Deer." Their antlers and velvet antlers are very precious, and traditional Chinese medicine considers them to have the effect of nourishing yin and tonifying yang. Deer are gentle by nature, and their fur changes with the seasons. In spring, it is reddish-brown with beautiful spots. In summer, it is brown. In autumn, it turns brownish-tea. When it turns burnt-tea, the spots gradually appear as well, but when does turn dark purple, the spots become less visible. In summer, deer live in deep mountains, and move to the foothills in winter. In late autumn, when maple leaves turn red, stags call out to hinds. Around April and May, they give birth in lush grassy areas near streams. The fawns are reddish-brown with white spots. Deer are herbivores, similar to giraffes. They move very quickly. If they encounter a predator, the stags will face them with their antlers, and the hinds will kick the enemy with their front legs. Deer antlers are replaced once every February or March, like an annual herb, with new growth every year. The antlers of young deer do not have short branches. After about eight years, they have three branches. When antlers first grow in the spring, the round ends are covered with skin, called "velvet antlers." At first, they are reddish-brown, gradually turning black. The antlers are densely covered with blood vessels. As they age, the velvet antlers turn into hard antlers. When fully developed, the outside is dark brown skin, like the trunk of a tree. The antlers naturally fall off every February, so before they fall off, they are sawn off for use in medicine and carving tools. Usually, the end of October is the most appropriate time to saw off the antlers. However, the deer raised in Chinese pharmacies are sawn off before that time in order to harvest the velvet antlers.

Children's Corner

Ten Good Friends 179

— Tao Kun, Grade 4, Kunshan Lvjiabang Elementary School

If we humans didn't have a pair of hands, we wouldn't be able to do anything. It's like fish not being able to swim without fins, and birds not being able to fly without wings. Thanks to us having this pair of hands, we are not afraid of not being able to do anything. Farmers use this pair of hands to grow rice for us to eat. They also grow cotton for us to make clothes to wear. Workers also use their pair of hands to make all kinds of things for us to use. Even eating and dressing, or using various tools, all require their use. Ten fingers are working non-stop, so we have food to eat, clothes to wear, and places to live. If they ever went on strike together, we would inevitably suffer from cold and hunger. They are truly our best friends. We rely on them for life, and we cannot leave them for a moment.

Catching Butterflies (Picture Story) 180

— Wang Letian

(1) One day, Mao Mao was playing in the flower garden when suddenly a butterfly flew past him. He quickly tried to catch it with his hand, but he missed, and the flower butterfly flew away in fright. (2) Mao Mao turned around and saw a fishing net, so he used it to catch this beautiful flower butterfly. (3) Chasing and running, he had walked close to the lake. He only paid attention to what was above. (4) So, not paying attention, he was tripped by a small stone and rushed into the lake. The flower butterfly laughed and said, "Who told you to catch me! This time, I'm giving you a good lesson. Next time, will you bully small animals again?"

Water That Doesn't Sink 181

— Ren Jianjun

Little friends will find this topic quite strange. How can there be water that doesn't sink? But the fact is this: in the British town of Trethevy Quoit, the water there mostly contains about 40% salt content—because the town is famous for its salt production. The locals have built several swimming pools. Because of the high salt content, the density of the water is high, so people won't sink in it. In that water, you can do all sorts of things, read the newspaper, play ball, have a picnic: it's truly supreme happiness. Little friends! Are you envious?

Children's Novel

Little Drummer (6) 182

— Xin Qing

The little drummer replied, "Of course! Do you think I could avoid it?" He said earnestly, because this was the first time he had been injured, and he felt very honored. Otherwise, he never dared to speak in front of the senior major.

"At that time, I lowered my head and ran for my life, and also crouched down from time to time, but those Austrians had already seen me. If they hadn't injured me, I could have arrived twenty minutes earlier. Fortunately, I ran into a major from the general headquarters, and I handed him the letter. However, I still struggled to come back afterward. I was dying of thirst, and I was worried, fearing that I would delay important matters. I was roaring angrily, thinking that every minute of delay would be enough to send one of our men to their death. But I have done my best. I am satisfied. But Major, look, you yourself are bleeding!"

Indeed, blood was flowing from the senior major's injured hand because the bandage was not secure.

The little drummer hurriedly said, "Major, should I tighten the bandage for you? Let me help you."

The senior major gave his injured left hand to the little drummer, while using his right hand to help tighten the knot of the rope; but the little drummer had just propped himself up from the pillow when his face suddenly turned pale and he fell back down.

The senior major looked at him and quickly retracted his hand, saying, "Forget it! Forget it! Take care of yourself, don't worry about other people's business; you must know that if you don't take care of a minor injury, it may become irreversible in the future."

The little drummer shook his head.

The senior major looked at him very intently and said, "But you are so weak, mostly because of too much blood loss."

The little drummer smiled and said, "Too much blood loss? More than blood. Look!" Saying that, he opened the blanket covering his lower body.

The senior major was shocked and took a step back.

The child only had one leg; the left leg had been amputated above the knee. The place where it was cut was wrapped in cloth, stained with blood.

At this moment, a short, fat military doctor walked past. He pointed at the little drummer and said to the major, "Ah! Major, this is an unfortunate thing. This leg could have been preserved, but because he used too much force, it was inflamed, so it had to be amputated, but he was very brave, and never shed a tear or cried out in pain. When I was performing the surgery, I felt very proud, thinking that he is truly one of our Italian children! Truly, he is the seed of a hero!" After speaking, he walked away.

The senior major frowned his thick white eyebrows, looking at the little drummer, and covering him with the blanket. Unconsciously, he raised his hand and took off his military hat.

The little drummer cried out in surprise, "Major! What? Are you saluting me?"

The rough old soldier, who never said a gentle word to his subordinates, said in a gentle voice, "I am just a major, but you are a hero!" Saying that, he stretched out his arms, held the little drummer, and kissed him very sincerely. (The End)

Grain: Large Factories Dump Spot Flour 192

However, the current economic hardship cannot be denied. The sluggishness of actual sales and the slight decline in spot prices are ultimately constrained by the economy. Yesterday, large non-industry stockpiles were still actively buying. Foreign wheat also rose, and market prices could have stabilized after factory sales, but the market instead fell. Women's Corner

Whose Sin Is It? 200

— Luo Qiong

—On the Issue of Women's Decoration—

During this period of special economic depression in the world, international trade is declining, and the domestic market is shrinking to an extreme, which has led to the most common and serious problems in the world today. However, under this economic situation, the production and consumption of women's consumer goods in various countries can stand apart. For example, in the United States, "the money spent on decorating women's faces and bodies continues to be as lavish as before the economic panic - about 30 million yuan per week, 156 million yuan per year, more than twice the revenue of India" (A. Hurley, "Cosmetics and Female Beauty," New China, Vol. 3, No. 15). From the perspective of the "production of the U.S. cosmetics industry, the scale of production of all industrial sectors has shrunk during this recession, but only the cosmetics industry has not been affected" (quoted from the above magazine), this not only confirms that the domestic consumption of women's cosmetics in the United States has not declined, but also shows that the consumption of American cosmetics in countries such as Europe, which consume the most, has not decreased. Even in China, where the consumption of cosmetics is relatively small, in this extremely serious economic panic, according to the National Tariff Commission's conversation with reporters: "In the first half of the year, the import of perfume and powder, a women's consumer good, reached 558,770 yuan, which has not decreased compared to the same period last year" (Shen Bao, August 3, 1935). The consumption of women's cosmetics in the above countries has not decreased, which refers to the absolute value; if compared to the proportion of general commodities, it has undoubtedly increased compared to last year or the year before.

In the present time, when international trade in various countries is generally declining and people's purchasing power is generally shrinking, the fact that women's cosmetics are still relatively increasing is a noteworthy issue. Therefore, various explanations have been aroused for this problem, and the conclusion of these many different explanations is that the beautification of women is becoming increasingly high. Therefore, in this recession, they would rather tighten other consumption than reduce the decoration on their bodies. As a result, the manufacturers of snow cream and white jade cream, the beauty experts, the sellers of rubber weight loss belts and weight loss massage machines, and the authors of how to cultivate the lower abdomen are still surging and continue to obtain their fat profits.

This explanation, on the surface, is of course not without reason; unfortunately, it only grasps the phenomenon and does not see the essence. The relative increase in women's cosmetics cannot be explained by psychological reasons such as women's "innate love of beauty" and "particularly high beautificationism." We should seek its fundamental causes from the changes in the economic life of women at all levels. During this panic, the polarization of the general population is becoming increasingly significant; the so-called upper-class women, relying on the concentration of their masters' capital and the increase in profits, can of course continue to expand their consumption of cosmetics indefinitely.

More importantly, a large number of middle- and lower-class women cannot find normal work to maintain their simple and plain lives during this period of economic contraction and widespread unemployment panic. Since labor cannot be sold, women's special commodities have to be sold, from prostitutes, dancers, massage therapists, and receptionists all the way to vases, socialites, and even the so-called "socialites" and "ladies," selling their bodies in various ways, either openly or secretly, creating a particularly prosperous market for human flesh. These special commodities, like general commodities, encounter fierce competition during the panic, so they have to use more beautiful decorations and larger advertisements to attract customers in order to sell. In order to obtain the necessities of life, these many women have to "fall into" the decadent life of injuring customs and morals, "using thick powder and enchanting clothes to beautify themselves as much as possible in order to win the favor of customers." Therefore, their "tightening other consumption and unwillingness to reduce facial decoration" is of the same significance as the hard-working farmers would rather starve and save a little money to buy seeds and fertilizer. Because if not, even this little "tightened" means of livelihood would be impossible to obtain!

It is easy to see here that the rise of women's beautificationism and the relative increase in the production and consumption of women's cosmetics are the results of the polarization of women's economic life, reflecting a very serious economic panic and hiding a very tragic and widespread sale of the body. Therefore, women's gorgeous clothes are completely built on the existing economic structure. If we think that women's heavy makeup is due to a natural love of beauty or a desire for vanity, and in turn condemn women, then we have not only failed to grasp the core of the problem, but also covered up the serious root of the problem. We oppose women's heavy makeup; however, we are convinced that this "injury customs and morals" behavior is not the sin of women themselves, but an inevitable thing created by the unreasonable social system. Under this system, women are not only slaughtered, but also "lambs" who "suffer for others."

Where is Paradise? 201

— Bai Ping

——The Experiences of a Girl from the Jiliang Institute——

Through a chance opportunity, I stayed for a few days in a Jiliang Institute in the Japanese Concession. I had the chance to chat with many of the girls there. Among them, Aihua was the most pitiful. Her story is briefly described below:

According to Aihua's own account: In the spring of her ninth year, her father passed away, and her mother went out to work as a hired hand in the countryside. Her eleven-year-old brother worked as a cowherd in a poor family in a nearby village. Aihua was sent to a woman in a neighboring village, known as a "female tiger," to be a child bride. From the moment she entered that door, her life became that of a beast of burden, constantly scolded while working! Besides cooking and laundry every day, she was often sent to the mountains to collect firewood. Poisonous snakes bit her hands and face; thorns painfully pricked her skin. Upon returning home, not only did she have no one to confide in, but she was sometimes beaten or forced to go hungry for returning too late or collecting too little firewood. Her husband was an idiot who was already fifteen years old but spent his days playing. Aihua had to serve him in everything.

She endured this kind of life for more than three years. As she gradually came to understand things, she felt that the abuse was unbearable, and her idiot husband made her future seem bleak. One autumn night, she quietly left this tiger's den, this living hell, alone. She walked and walked, hoping that in the city she could find some work, support herself, or perhaps even find her mother.

City H was a bustling and scenic city. When she arrived, it was exactly seven o'clock in the morning. Everything she heard and saw felt new and interesting. Aimlessly, she didn't know where to go, so she wandered nervously around the intersection. At this moment, a policeman suddenly appeared, grabbed her without explanation, and dragged her away. She trembled with fear, crying and begging, but no one paid attention to her. As a result, she was dragged into the detention center. At this time, she felt regret, anger, and panic. The bitterness in her heart was indescribable. Aside from crying, she couldn't say a word. After three or four days, and transfers to two or three places, she was sent to this Jiliang Institute. Inside were sisters of similar age and supervisors who never left their sides. Her clothing, food, and housing were also taken care of. She thought this was paradise on earth and that she could learn to read, work, and live a stable life. Little did she know that the reality was completely different from what she expected. The supervisors' gentle attitude at the beginning turned into a ferocious and menacing expression. They scolded and鞭策 her all day long, making her live in constant fear. At the same time, the food was not nutritious enough, and a dozen people were crammed into one room. Air and sunlight were naturally out of the question, and they were confined all year round, not allowed to step outside. Her heart was full of sorrow, with no one to confide in. After two years of this, Aihua was already pale and as thin as a rail. Her tuberculosis had reached the second stage.

Fortunately, a compassionate supervisor came later. She sympathized with the girls, especially Aihua. Knowing that she had tuberculosis, she tried to treat her and provide her with nutrition. Only then did Aihua taste what people called kindness. Unexpectedly, this compassionate supervisor was dismissed by the later director in less than a month. When Aihua heard this news, she felt extremely sad because she would soon lose this motherly supervisor. She cried, she cried bitterly! Just as she was crying sadly, she suddenly heard a thunderous roar, and at the same time, she was struck three or four times on the back with an iron-like fist. Poor girl! Her head was dizzy, her heart ached, and she rolled on the ground, like a lamb about to be slaughtered. She coughed violently, spitting out a large pool of blood. Wanting to resist, she was threatened by the iron fist and dared not move. Later, she learned that this iron-fisted man was the brother of the director of the institute. Because he hated her emotional display of farewell, he struck her with his iron fist. From then on, Aihua fell ill in bed, living a life of suffering from illness.

Women's Issues Lecture

Section 5: Women on the Eve of World War II 202

— Jun Hui

Since the panic on the New York Stock Exchange in the autumn of 1929, the capitalist world has begun to embark on a path of despair and darkness. Many scholars, capitalists, speculators, and political commentators believed in the principle of economic cycles, advocated the possibility of economic recovery, and longed for the return of the golden age of capitalism! However, the ruthless reality shattered their illusions. It had been six years since the panic erupted, and not only was there no hope of ending it, but it had spread widely to the world, grasping everyone's hearts more deeply. If panic is a flood, then the people in the capitalist world are all drifting and struggling in this flood. As a result, countries are all studying ways to save themselves, trying to rescue their own countries from the muddy currents of panic!

But where is the way to save oneself! There is only one way, which is to sacrifice other countries to prosper one's own country—war! We know that after this panic, a "live or die" war has already begun between countries. This is the so-called tariff war and currency war. Now these economic wars are turning into wars of poison gas and bombs. In Manchuria in the East, the first battle has already passed. In Africa in the West, a massacre is being prepared! In this way, the terrible god of war that people curse has finally poured down on our heads! Now is the eve of the great destruction of mankind! People are trembling before this terrible god of war!

However, on the eve of this Second World War, we women cannot help but recall the painful past of the First Imperialist War. Therefore, we cannot but prepare to cope with the inevitable disaster of tomorrow!

Women in various capitalist countries have already experienced various kinds of suffering during the gestation period of this Second World War. In order to alleviate the unemployment panic, governments openly deprived women of their right to move. In order to increase the number of citizens who would become cannon fodder in the war, women were asked to give birth to children at home. In order to make women soldiers in the rear during the war, women were given military training. In this way, governments regarded women as necessary supplies for preparing for war, and placed them under the control of the state and even the military!

We often see in newspapers the preparations for the coming war by women in various countries. The most prominent of these are the women of Japan and Germany. The Great Japan National Defense Women's Association, organized in 1932, had a total of 1,688,424 members by the end of April this year. It is said that the association is developing very rapidly, and now there are branches in the Kwantung Leased Territory and Manchuria. It is completely under the guidance of the military and will carry out the tasks that women can do in the war.

Secondly, since Hitler came to power in Germany, the country has been preparing for war. Since the recent announcement of rearmament, women throughout the country have also had to assume the responsibility of national defense. According to the latest Berlin dispatch; "There are now six million German women who have received considerable training to serve the country in times of war. In addition, there are twice as many women who are currently undergoing training, so that the country can use their capabilities once something happens, in line with the new national conscription system." "... About six million German women are currently joining air defense associations and aeronautical societies, and others aged between eighteen and fifty are also engaged in more general activities. In short, all German women are registered by the National Socialist Party for use when the country needs them." (Damei Evening Post, August 3rd)

This situation is the same in all capitalist countries at present, especially in Italy recently, which is mobilizing the people of the whole country, sending men to the African front, and incorporating women into the labor force of military supplies industry, as in the First World War.

But here, there are two points that we women must pay attention to. The first point is that the war in capitalist society, although it raises the banner of "patriotism" or "national survival" on the surface, is in essence something launched by a few capitalists in order to obtain their commodity markets and to obtain huge profits. The result of the war, even if victory is achieved, is only the victory of a few capitalists. Most of the people who participate in the war are either cannon fodder or have illusory joy! Especially women, no matter whether they win or lose, cannot achieve fundamental liberation. The experience of the First World War tells us that women in both victorious and defeated countries only lost their husbands and children, and aggravated the tragic lives of women! Therefore, we should stand up and resolutely oppose war. The second point is that since we have recognized the nature of modern war, then we must actively obtain women's own liberation in the war. We know that in the First World War, the women of the Soviet Union actively participated in this liberation war, and as a result, they achieved final victory!

"Postscript" In the eighteen lectures, I have very briefly described the lives of women in various major eras and societies. This may be said to be a small history of women's lives, and I want to conclude it here as the first part of this lecture. Starting from the nineteenth lecture, I will specifically talk about the real problems such as women's problems and women's liberation movements raised in this historical development, but because the lecturer has limited ability and various restrictions, I cannot live up to the readers' expectations. I am very sorry! I hope readers will give me unreserved criticism.

The Life of Boat Girls on Nanhu Lake in Jiaxing 203

— Guan Ting

Nanhu Lake in Jiaxing, Zhejiang, also known as Mandarin Duck Lake, has very beautiful scenery. The famous Misty Rain Tower stands in the center of the lake, and is also attached with many pavilions, terraces, and towers, which reflect each other. There are also many historical sites that can be commemorated, so it is often crowded with tourists and extremely lively. Only because the Misty Rain Tower is surrounded by water on all sides, and there is no land route to pass through, people who go to visit must take a boat in order to cross over.

The boat rowers are generally young women, the older ones are less than thirty years old, and the younger ones are only thirteen or fourteen years old. There are generally two on each boat, and tourists call them boat girls.

These boat girls, in order to attract tourists, all put on rouge and powder, and their attire strives to be fashionable, preferring to have something to wear without being able to save on food. Generally, people always come out in the afternoon and evening, so these boat girls don't come out much in the morning, either resting at home or washing the boat clean on the boat. Once it comes to the afternoon, they all put on heavy makeup and come out to solicit business.

After they come out, they go to solicit customers along the street. Even when the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway train arrives at Jiaxing Station, they actually run to the station from afar to pick up customers.

"Rowing the boat? "I'll take you! I'll take you to Misty Rain Tower to have fun! "Your boat is clean, can I take you there?"... These kinds of words are the terms they use when soliciting tourists. If they see the tourist nod in agreement, they are very happy and lead the way with a smile, leading the tourist to their boat; if the guest does not agree, they pucker their lips at that guest and go to solicit someone else.

But they are all very kind. If you get on their boat, the hospitality is very thoughtful. When the famous Nanhu water chestnuts or lotus roots are on the market, they will take out peeled water chestnut meat or sugar-pickled lotus roots to offer to the guests, but if you eat a plate of their water chestnut meat or lotus roots, in addition to the boat fare, you should at least reward them with two dimes.

Contribution to the Newspaper

Going Home (Continued) 204

— Su Hong

As usual, Xiuzhen returned from the mountain after collecting firewood, her face a little red, but mostly green. As she turned from behind the house, her sister-in-law was bending over to pull up mustard greens, piles of dirt turning over with the roots of the vegetables.

Grandfather stood next to her, picking up small stones and throwing them aside from time to time, muttering to himself:

—Really, you think I'm dealing rice with you. Look how hard the soil is on this piece of land, all stones. If I were to use this piece of land, it wouldn't be enough even if I spent ten days removing all the stones and turning over the soil. You don't have to set it up this year. Next spring, take two boats of lake mud and spread it on top, then you can grow vegetables.

After grandfather left, her sister-in-law looked at the vegetables, looked at the empty land, stood there blankly for a while, then went to the kitchen to get a kitchen knife and sat on a low stool, chopping vegetable heads.

Xiu Zhen put the firewood down under the porch, and her mother instructed her:

—Xiuzhen! Spread the firewood out a bit to let it air out."

Xiu Zhen entered the door and took off her straw shoes, and her mother sighed:

—The vegetable garden has already been pawned! Alas! She sighed. "To pull up such small mustard greens... It always can't be kept... This piece of land..."

Her sister-in-law cooked a large pot of vegetable porridge. When it was time to eat lunch, she put the child on the stool and said with a smile to Granny Youfu, who delivered the money for reciting the Buddha's name:

—Look! My sister is helping me with housework! She fetches firewood for me every day." Turning to Xiu Zhen:

—Sister! Eat porridge, I cooked thick porridge." She changed her tone and said to the child, "Little one! Sit over a bit, don't soil your aunt!"

Granny Youfu handed the copper coins to her mother:

—Old Mrs. Zonggui asked me to send the money for reciting the Buddha's name. She said it's seventy-two in total. The fourteen you borrowed last time have been deducted, so here are fifty-eight copper coins. Count them!" Saying this, her eyes glanced at the thick porridge on the stove.

The compassionate mother knew that Granny Youfu was the same as herself, and that she was alone, with no children, living alone in a thatched shed, and that she was always able to get through the days by reciting the Buddha's name. When she got the chance to recite the Buddha's name, she ate two meals a day, and sometimes only one, so she was always walking from house to house, waiting for people to eat, and asking for a little oil.

—Aunt Youfu, have a bowl, it's hot." The mother brought over a bowl of porridge.

The sister-in-law's eyes darted sideways at the bowl of porridge that was being handed over. Although she didn't say anything, her heart ached, she thought: "This bowl of porridge! It's that pawned piece of land. Eating one more bowl of porridge means one less piece of land." The child spilled a little porridge, and she took the opportunity to vent her anger, the chopsticks drumming on the child's head, rattling away: "Little devil! No eating, noisy eating, there is eating, not eating properly."

Granny Youfu ate like a tiger devouring a butterfly. As soon as her stomach was a little full, she began to talk about this and that:
