Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Amateur Ramblings

The Fighting Nation and the Fighting Individual 206

— Kuo Qing

The process of life is the history of battle, which is the common principle of all living things, and of course human beings are no exception. All living things must survive, they resist the oppression of natural cold, heat, hunger, and thirst, and fight with nature, resist the persecution of similar living things, and fight with other lives, and they constantly maintain their lives in the process of fighting, so they live in the world. Human beings, in their fundamental way of life, are exactly the same. They fight with nature, obtain living resources from the struggle of production, avoid various oppressions of cold, heat, hunger, and thirst, and they also fight with ordinary lives, defending against the harm of other creatures to them, using and overcoming domesticated creatures for their own use, becoming the victorious dominator in the war. He also fights with human beings themselves in a certain stage of evolution, striving for the survival interests and rights of individuals and the social groups whose interests are the same as his. From this, it can be seen that there is no life without struggle, and no living without fighting.

Although human beings and ordinary living things all live in battle in the same way, the fighting methods of ordinary living things are mostly individual direct response forms of fighting, simply determining their direct fighting methods according to the environment. A fierce tiger fights back with teeth and claws, and a sheep simply runs away when chased. Although a cat knows to lie still when catching a mouse, waiting for its opponent not to know it, and then suddenly jump to catch the mouse, this is still only limited to the instinctive impulse of fighting. Human beings are different, because human beings have a very complex social life, so their battles are carried out through many curves, and they must see the intricate relationship of the complex environment everywhere, distinguish it consciously, and even know how to choose and plan various fighting methods and strategies to win. Therefore, when active on the front line of human life and fighting for life, one must strictly study tactics and strategies.

In a broad sense, human beings also have their tactics and strategies for fighting against nature, because human beings themselves, in terms of their own ability, have neither the strength of fierce tigers nor their sharp claws and teeth, nor the flying skills of birds in the air, nor the running ability of good horses and cunning rabbits, so when he fights with physical strength and instinct alone, he can't even be considered a strong person in the biological group, let alone conquer the great forces of nature. However, human beings have eventually become the king of creatures and the conqueror of nature, which is because they have various ingenious techniques of fighting and certain tactics of winning. These fighting techniques of human beings are the production techniques of human beings. All scientific developments, as human organs themselves extend, deform, and improve, are artificial organs, such as machines and all production tools, and even the methods of engaging in production using these tools, are the production techniques of human beings, and the techniques of fighting on the lifeline of human life. Human beings not only have these particularly ingenious techniques for fighting against nature, but also have certain strategies, which is to use nature itself to subdue nature. Although human beings themselves are weak animals, they can overcome nature by using excellent combat techniques and strategies that use nature to subdue nature in combat. This is the tactics and strategies that ordinary creatures do not know to study on the lifeline of life.

In social life, because human beings are divided into several layers of groups in a certain stage of social evolution, and even divided into individual people to live in different positions and interests, the battle between people is also universally developed in such a society. Human beings live in a society of individualistic and self-interested concepts and separate groups, and there are various types and forms of struggle at all times. Without struggle, there is no survival, so this kind of tactics and strategies in life are more complex in form, and they are naturally developed and become necessary for each group and individual to study. In fact, it is often obvious that in a society where individual economic systems exist, the most prominent is first of all the separate groups based on ethnic relations and political and economic governance, that is, between ethnic nation-states, which are always in a state of mutual opposition and struggle, which has produced the military, political, economic and other diplomatic tactics and strategies of ethnic nation-states. Whoever does not study these tactics and strategies, whoever is not good at using them, can cause diplomatic failure if it is small, and even ruin the survival of his nation and country if it is large. Especially in the era of the emergence of modern large nation-states, all citizens are brought into this competition and participate in the battle based on the tactics and strategies of the rulers.

In every ethnic nation-state, there are also conflicts between unequal social strata, forming the opposition between ununified groups, and fierce struggles occur from time to time. In terms of various political, economic, and social facilities, each has different political views for the sake of the interests of their own group in life. Each social group forms its own political party and fights with each other to win the leadership of the country. Therefore, in elections, in all state organs, in parliament, and even for all political orders and social facilities, each has its own political tactics and strategies. Moreover, its political party is dedicated to creating these tactics and strategies, and leading its group to use these tactics and strategies to fight. Therefore, in modern society, all people are also involved in the study and execution of these tactical and strategic tactics of private group interests.

As for individual private individuals? For the sake of life, in this society where individualism and self-interest develop, one must always plan for one's own life and interests and study tactics and strategies. For example, many people advance in the advancing era and retreat in the retreating era, and some even strongly violate the dominance of reason and change everything about themselves, making themselves seem like two different people. This can be said to be a kind of tactics and strategies carried out entirely for the sake of personal living interests.

Human beings cannot but fight to live, and they must study tactics and strategies anytime and anywhere to fight, so we do not oppose studying tactics and strategies anytime and anywhere, and even recognize that this is a necessity in life in society. However, in a divided world, we can only admit that the study of tactics and strategies by the weak is appropriate, because they simply cannot survive if they do not fight and do not study combat tactics and strategies. As for the future world, its struggle is directed solely at nature, so what human beings need to develop is science and production technology, that is, they need to study only the tactics and strategies of fighting against nature, and the tactics and strategies of fighting between people are not necessary in life.

Life Guidance

How to Live a Wandering Life? 207

— Jianqun

In a wandering life, economic pressure, physical fatigue, and emotional distress are inevitable. However, if you can understand the meaning of "wandering" and know how to live a wandering life, you can reduce some of the suffering. Therefore, a wanderer, especially one who is just starting out, should learn the skills of wandering and pay attention to various subtleties. The saying "even begging requires a teacher" illustrates this point.

Some people are driven by life's pressures and have no choice but to travel around in search of employment. However, "traveling around" should not be aimless; it should be a planned "reliance." Before going to a certain place, you must ascertain the personnel relationships there. You should have at least a 50% certainty of securing a job. If you go there rashly, relying solely on new pursuits, problems are bound to arise. Even if the outcome doesn't lead to a dead end, the losses incurred will be significant. In reality, you must investigate the living conditions and the number of personal friends in that location in advance. This will facilitate planning your finances and prevent you from being stranded in a foreign land, wasting money and time, should employment issues arise.

Secondly, travel expenses are also a common difficulty for wanderers. Sometimes, opportunities to find employment may arise elsewhere, but due to a lack of funds, the opportunity is lost. Therefore, you should familiarize yourself with the transportation options. As far as I know, the "extra-stop trains" and "freight cars" on the Pinghan Railway do not charge fares. If you are in Hankou and urgently need to go to Beiping, you don't need to delay raising travel funds. You can take this cheap transportation, even if it's a bit uncomfortable. Also, the fares for fast and slow trains differ significantly. For example, from Shanghai to Nanjing, a special express train costs more than three yuan and seventy cents, while a fourth-class seat on a slow train costs only two yuan. The seating is sometimes not very crowded, and the delay is only about three hours. If you want to save money, it's best to take the slow train. However, you must pay close attention because there are many thieves on slow trains. They don't dare to venture into the special express trains, which are heavily guarded by military police, to steal from wealthy passengers. Instead, they target the poor friends riding the slow trains. Once they have an opportunity, they will not hesitate to take your only possession, regardless of your poverty. There are naturally many ways to prevent this, but you must understand the subtleties involved to avoid wasting effort. Before the ship sets sail and after it anchors are times when thieves "show their skills." You should watch your luggage and only relax after the ship has set sail. When riding a train, pay special attention to the first stop, as thieves often steal things while passengers are in confusion shortly after the train departs. They then get off at the first stop and return to the city. This is most evident on the Pinghan Railway because there are more thieves there than elsewhere.

During the journey, you may want to make a few honest friends. This will allow you to learn more about the destination, have someone to look after you along the way, and pass the time while relieving your sorrow and enlivening your mood. However, speak sincerely and avoid being frivolous, or others may mistake you for a "drifter" or a "traveling hustler." Before arriving at your destination, inquire about the names, addresses, and room rates of local hotels and inns to avoid confusion and unnecessary losses. You should also be aware of the conditions at the docks and the regulations for handling luggage; otherwise, being "gouged" and disrupting your budget can be quite a blow!

Wanderers should learn the languages of various regions in advance, at least enough to speak a few everyday phrases. This not only makes it easier to find employment but also

Page 23

reduces many difficulties. Of course, learning the languages of different provinces cannot be achieved in a short period, but learning a few common essential phrases is easy. For example, rickshaws are called "yellow package cars" in Shanghai, "rubber skins" in Tianjin, simply "cars" in Chengdu, "foreign cars" in Qingdao and Beiping, cigarettes are called "tobacco sticks" in the north, "tobacco sons" in Guangzhou, and "paper cigarettes" in Sichuan... As long as you can say the names, you can reduce a lot of trouble. Even if your pronunciation is not perfect, others will still know you are a foreigner, but they won't dare to think of you as a newcomer.

As for the housing problem in a wandering life, it depends on your status and financial capabilities. It should also be appropriate for your activities and the social circles you frequent. If the friend you are "relying on" is a high-ranking official who cares about face, and the job you are seeking is also high-end, and the people you associate with are all elegant, then you have to stay in a mid-range or higher hotel to avoid being looked down upon for being poor, even if your travel funds are a little tight. However, you should also consider whether the job is reliable, or you will suffer later! In fact, wanderers do not have lavish social lives. For financial reasons, it is best to find affordable accommodation. If you want to live in Beiping for a month or two, it is best to find a suitable apartment that includes meals for about thirteen or fourteen yuan per month. Tea and water are readily available, and the service is attentive (there are many such apartments in both the east and west of the city), which is suitable for the status and tastes of wandering intellectuals. If you want to stay longer, you can rent your own house. A medium-sized one costs only two or three yuan per month. You can buy meal tickets for six or seven yuan per month. Living in Shanghai is about one-third more expensive than in Beiping. Taking apartments as an example, room and board together cost at least twenty-two or twenty-three yuan. If you are staying for a month or two, it is more cost-effective to rent a house. In remote areas, you can rent a small room in the attic for five yuan or a back room for three or four yuan. You can eat two meals at a workers' restaurant for two mao a day, which is about twelve yuan for the whole month. However, it is not easy to rent a house in Guangzhou or Hankou, and you also need family members and a guarantor. Therefore, people wandering in these two places can only stay in small inns. (In Guangzhou, in addition to the lavish "hotels," there are also "student residences" that are also used for average tourists. These lodgings cost about sixteen to twenty yuan per month). In short, the cost of living varies in different places, and the local conditions are different. Wanderers should investigate in advance and then drift in a planned way, to avoid unexpected difficulties in life.

In addition, common sense is also something that old wanderers should pay attention to. Here are a few examples. First, China's monetary system is extremely chaotic. Each province and county has several or even dozens of types of "currency" in circulation, but the area of circulation is limited. The "currency" used here often becomes useless in other provinces. The double hao coins commonly used in Shanghai are clearly made in Guangdong, but they are not accepted in Guangdong (where they are called "old hao coins" and new hao coins with the image of Mr. Sun Yat-sen are used). The hao coins of Nanjing are the same as those circulating in Shanghai, but those from the years 1920 and 1921 are not accepted. Sichuan's silver dollars—called "Sichuan version"—are permanently ineligible to leave the Kui Pass because they are said to be of poor quality and insufficient content. If you don't understand these "subtleties" and take "Sichuan version" to other provinces or hao coins from 1920 and 1921 to Nanjing, and you are short on travel funds, you may be in danger of starving. Second, customs inspections in Hong Kong are particularly strict, and "gouging" is especially severe. Fresh goods are taxed or confiscated, and even bringing more than one tin of cigarettes (preferably with the lid cut open) is subject to tax and a fine. If you don't understand these situations and bring a tin of cigarettes from Shanghai to Guangzhou as a gift for a friend, you may be unlucky! Third, the food on ocean liners is bad (it has stones and is gritty) and there are no vegetables. If possible, prepare some dry food before you leave. However, it is different when taking a train. There is food and drink to buy at every stop along the way, and it is fresh and cheap. If you prepare it in advance, you are just doing something foolish!

Philosophy Lecture

From Positivism to Pragmatism 208

— Zhuoran

Positivism is the philosophical system of Comte, while pragmatism is the philosophical system of James in the United States. Although these two philosophical systems have different points in terms of name and formal content, they have many things in common in terms of general ideological principles. From the perspective of external form, both are based on experience and practice, becoming a philosophy of empiricism. In Comte's view, the ultimate goal of human thought and what he can know is only the positive empirical facts and the laws they reveal. The noumenon of things is unknowable, and what is known is only the phenomenal things. However, knowing the laws of phenomenal things, they should serve mankind. The work of science is to empirically verify these things and laws, and to synthesize these things and laws, so that it can be transformed into a tool for serving mankind, and recognition and knowledge have value and are worthy of attention here. What about James' pragmatism? It is also roughly the same in this kind of thinking, not focusing on abstract theoretical debates, but focusing on the verification of real situations, and only in practice can right and wrong be determined. Therefore, the cognition and disputes of all truths are boundless and endless, and no results or values can be obtained there. What is truly valuable is only practicality. Everything that is practical is right, and vice versa is worthless and wrong. Therefore, pragmatism is also a philosophy of experience and hard work to a certain extent.

However, after positivism opposed all beliefs and fantasies of abstract thinking and principles, it stepped into the realm of Kantian agnosticism and Humean phenomenology. Because it believes that it is impossible to enter the scope of the noumenon, and the noumenon itself is unknowable. What we can know and should know is limited to the things in the phenomenal world. Even if things have a true essence, in terms of practical benefits, it may be completely irrelevant or even useless to human progress. When positivism reaches such a theoretical scope, it further includes in its philosophy the denial of the meaning of objective truth, because it believes that what can serve mankind is good, and there is no objective and absolute truth principle, and there is no unified entity based on the noumenon. It denies the possibility of cognition of the noumenon of things, denies the possibility of the existence of objective essence and truth, and takes the actual interests of human beings or its parts and even individuals as the premise to determine the value of everything. This is another form of human-centered philosophy. What about pragmatism? It also believes that all debates on principles and principles are empty and cannot reach ultimate differences, and even says that if differences cannot be verified in the practical scope, it is better to say that they are the same, without right or wrong. Therefore, we cannot know the essence of truth, or we can say that there is no truth at all. It believes that principles and systems are difficult to achieve, and only concrete things, achievable phenomenal expressions, actions and facts, etc., are what it pays attention to. True things are only in line with practicality, and practicality is based on human interests. Therefore, it not only believes that truth is difficult to distinguish, difficult to speak, and difficult to know, but also that it is worthless. To judge things, it is only necessary to rely on their actual manifestations, only to weigh right and wrong based on the practical interests of each person in their practice, without the need for any other principles and standards, so that disputes can be reconciled. In this way, pragmatism also contains agnosticism of things themselves. Its experience stops at the realm of phenomena and subjectivity, and does not reach the other shore of things. It is a denial of truth.

Originally, agnosticism of the thing-in-itself was Kant's dualistic philosophy. Because on the one hand, he admitted the existence of the noumenon of things, but in the sense that this noumenon of things is unknowable, he regarded the phenomena we feel and the consciousness reflected by these phenomena on our subjectivity as things that cannot completely identify and express the thing itself. Since the subjective acquisition of things cannot fundamentally express external things, these things are nothing but the products and illusions of the subjective mind, because it cannot be used as an explanation of external things, nor is it something produced by external things. Therefore, everything in the psychology is parallel to external things, unrelated and independently existing. Regardless of whether Kant simply admitted that the things in subjective consciousness were just psychological fabrications, the necessary logic of that agnosticism of the thing-in-itself is like this. Positivists and pragmatists do not know at all that the subjective depends on the objective, that thinking is produced by reality, and that everything in psychology is a reflection of the external reality. Therefore, it must explain external things to a certain extent. The progress of human knowledge means that the reflection of the outside world is becoming more and more realistic. The reason why science is science is also because it recognizes external things. External things are not unknowable, but their secrets are constantly being revealed. External things are truly existing, and knowledge of them is gradually acquired. Then, no matter how the outside world changes, this change is also the change of objective reality itself. Human beings obtain the reality of change from change, which is still objective truth. Truth is not only existent but also absolute in its objectivity. It is relative in its change due to the change of its own objective reality, but this cannot be used to deny the existence of truth. If it is said that there is no truth or truth is worthless, then the outside world is not real, and it is meaningless and worthless. Positivists and pragmatists advocate the importance of practice, which is correct from the standpoint of human beings themselves. Therefore, it is not impossible in principle to pay attention to everything that is practical and can promote human progress. However, human beings and their interests appeared very late, and they are only a part of nature, so it cannot be said that there is no universe and no truth outside of human beings, and that truth and the world are over when human beings do not exist. Moreover, the establishment of human self-demands and concepts also takes root in the external world of nature and society, and cannot be explained from human nature. If the opinions of positivism and pragmatism continue to develop, and objective truth and right and wrong are denied, then every person has his practical views, and various societies and individuals also have different practical viewpoints. Then, the guns and cannons of imperialism and the knives of oppressors are practical to them, and their oppression and slaughter become reasonable truths. On the contrary, the resistance of opponents is more reasonable. This not only becomes a theory that helps the wicked to do evil, but also its contradictions are really unsolvable.

If we examine the era in which positivism and pragmatism occurred, then they were after the establishment of modern society, when most people could not be satisfied with their original ideals, and thus society had a tendency to pursue other new ideals. Therefore, they had to come out to deny that the admiration of new ideals was reasonable, and call on everyone to be content with the status quo in the experiment, and even support things that had practical value for a few people. Of course, when it developed to the end, they themselves were disappointed with their society, and in the turmoil, they needed compromise and reconciliation. Therefore, on the one hand, they were pessimistic about the impossibility of the yearning for objective truth, and on the other hand, they had to find ways to obliterate the rationality of debate and fighting for truth, in order to live in the present reality and make people not go beyond the practical viewpoints of life trivia and partial events, and reconcile the existing contradictions and stop disputes. However, the progress of society has made it impossible for most human beings to seek any real interests. In the facts of real daily life, they cannot find any practical meaning for their own interests. The evidence of the situation only proves their pain. Therefore, the pursuit of new truth cannot be stopped, and this philosophy still cannot save the poor. Let some people promote the immediate real interests and temporality, oppose the pursuit of truth and move forward, and even deny that there is so-called objective truth. I am afraid it will not be of much use!

Outlying Postal Agency

Daughter Red 209

— Liu Yuqing

Shaoxing Correspondence

Shaoxing is not a very big county in Zhejiang Province, but from a historical point of view, it has always been famous throughout the country. The reason for its fame is, on the one hand, that during the Qing Dynasty, the footprints of "Shaoxing counselors" could be found in government offices everywhere, so the place became famous because of the people; on the other hand, it was because of the popularity of Shaoxing wine, and this small county became even more famous in the world. Regarding "Shaoxing counselors," there is no need to recall the past and say more nonsense. What I want to talk about is the booming and once prosperous Shaoxing winemaking.

There is no scenery or famous attractions in Shaoxing. If tourists from other places come here to explore and seek out hidden beauty, I guarantee that you will shake your head and sigh, shout "fooled" and go back. But if a person with a fondness for Li Bai comes here, I dare to guarantee that he will not want to go back. There are not many streets in Shaoxing, and there are no wide roads like in Shanghai, but the number of liquor stores accounts for 50 to 60 percent of all stores. As soon as you step on the street, all you see are signs with names such as "The Legacy of Taibai," "Chunyu Yishi," and "Liu Li Parking."

Since there are so many liquor stores here, the number of people who drink can be imagined. There are countless customers who like the style of Lu Xun's "Kong Yiji." Therefore, the layout of general liquor stores is also very casual because the "drunkard's intention" is indeed "in the wine." In a liquor store, in addition to a few tables and simple wine utensils, all you can see are wine jars. Even if they are busy with work, people who like to drink will still take time to sneak to the liquor store counter for a satisfying drink.

It is of course expected that Shaoxing people like to drink Shaoxing wine, but non-Shaoxing people also like to drink Shaoxing wine. This is why Shaoxing winemaking is superior to others. However, it can be said that there are places to make wine everywhere in China. So, why is Shaoxing wine so famous in the world? This is naturally for good reason. According to the analogy of winemakers: "Rice is the meat of wine, flour is the bone of wine, and water is the blood of wine." From this, we can see the importance of water in wine. It is said that Shaoxing wine became famous because of the help of Jian Lake water. Jian Lake is about three miles from Shaoxing and was built by Prefect Ma of the Han Dynasty. Although Jian Lake itself was later abandoned, many of the tributaries it formed have not changed. The most beautiful water in them is Qingti

How to Study History? 210

— Yu Fu

Shirakawa Hakumura said in his "Symbols of Torment": "The development of everything progresses from simple to complex. Therefore, to understand the essence of a thing, one must first trace its origin and look back to its most authentic and simple original state." Human life is also "progressing from simple to complex"; if there were no feudal-era agriculture and handicraft life, or even if there were no primitive-era crude and simple life of drinking blood, then mankind would never be able to enjoy modern "civilized" life. Therefore, if we want to understand the present and predict the future, we must know where the present and even the future come from, in other words, we must study the past history.

Furthermore, "people are both the authors and performers of their own drama," so people not only live in society, but also are historical animals, "performers and authors of their own history." Our study of history is to study the past activities and creations of mankind, and at the same time, it is also to create the future history with the understanding of the past, and move towards the path of light. Therefore, as long as it is not a person who lives in a muddle, but a person who lives soberly and seriously, he must study the past, understand the present, and create his personal life in the creation of human history, that is, he must understand the past history, accept the experience of human past life, and thus consciously participate in the work of human creation of history, and play the most important role in promoting the progress of history on the stage of history.

So, how to study history? In the past, many of our historians only recorded the changes of dynasties, the words and deeds of the royal family, the life-long careers of heroes and their birth and death dates, while the lives of ordinary people and the changes in social economy were not their concerns. Dealing with history in this way can at most only know some facts about those upper-class figures who appeared on the stage of history, and is still at a loss about the past history. Therefore, our study of history cannot adopt this unscientific and useless method. We must find the causal law of historical development, examine the organizational forms of human society, and explore the driving force of social evolution, historical changes and progress, because only in this way can we reflect the causal law of objective historical development and change as our subjective law of historical research, so as to study history with this scientific method that conforms to history, and truly understand the past and create the future. Here we can draw this famous formula!

"In the social production of their life, people enter into definite, necessary relations, independent of their will, namely relations of production which correspond to a definite stage of development of their material productive forces. The totality of these relations of production constitutes the economic structure of society, the real foundation on which legal and political superstructures arise and to which definite forms of social consciousness correspond. The mode of production of material life conditions the general process of social, political and intellectual life. It is not the consciousness of men that determines their being, but, on the contrary, their social being that determines their consciousness. At a certain stage of development, the material productive forces of society come into conflict with the existing relations of production or – what is but a legal expression for the same thing – with the property relations within which they have hitherto operated. From forms of development of the productive forces these relations turn into their fetters. Then begins an era of social revolution. With the change of the economic foundation the entire immense superstructure is more or less rapidly transformed....”

According to this, we can see that the organization of society is based on economy, and the development and changes of history also appear with the development and changes of social economy. The political changes, rebellions and wars, changes in social thought, and changes of dynasties in the past history are all inseparably related to the social economic form, and are not absolutely accidental phenomena. As for the heroes who appeared on the stage of history, they all emerged due to the needs of society on a certain economic foundation, and they were definitely not the stars descending to the earth. Therefore, when we study history, we should not only know the changes of dynasties, the facts of rebellions and wars, but also understand the social roots of their occurrence; for those heroes, we should not only know their careers and living conditions, but also understand how they were produced under what social conditions, and what role they played in human society. Because only in this way can we truly understand history, understand the characters in history; so that we will not become vulgar historians who know what happened but do not know why.

Take the history of China as an example. In the past history of China, the most noteworthy historical facts, such as Qin Shihuang's annexation of the six countries, his policies of abolishing the feudal system and establishing counties and prefectures and burning books and burying Confucian scholars, Wang Mang's usurpation of the throne, and his revival of the well-field system, as well as the Huang Chao Rebellion in the Tang Dynasty, Wang Anshi's reform in the Ming Dynasty, the Wuxu Reform in the Qing Dynasty and even the Xinhai Revolution... and other major events were all produced under certain social systems and economic conditions, and were by no means accidental phenomena without roots. However, the historians of the past only recorded the process of these events, and did not investigate the root causes of them, so they did not make correct explanations of these historical facts; sometimes, they even did not hesitate to use their own prejudices and adopt the so-called "praise and criticism" method to unreasonably scold those characters who were not approved by them, such as Qin Shihuang, Wang Mang and even Wang Anshi and others, were often scolded by general moralists. But dealing with history in this way resulted in not only not knowing the reason of history, but also probably making the facts inexplicable. Look at our Twenty-Four Histories, probably none of them really explained history. Therefore, we must use new methods to study history and reorganize the social history of China. For us, all the facts in the past history are not only objectively existing, but also have certain social roots, so we must find the roots of those historical facts from the social point of view, so as to explain those historical facts. We neither laugh nor cry, and we do not adopt the "praise and criticism" method of the moralists, we just objectively study history and explain history from the social point of view. For example, Qin Shihuang's abolition of the feudal system and the establishment of counties and prefectures and burning books and burying Confucian scholars, which is generally scolded by moralists, but for us, for general scientific historical researchers, Qin Shihuang's unification of the world, breaking the situation of feudal division, and establishing a centralized government was due to the development of commercial capital, which is still progressive; as for Qin Shihuang's burying of Confucian scholars, it was burying those feudal students who opposed the new society and attempted to retreat, and did not bury all the scholars, in fact, the scholars of Xunzi's school at that time, such as Li Si, were not buried, so we cannot simply scold Qin Shihuang when studying history because we see Qin Shihuang's burning books

Continued from page five

Page 24

Page 25

The task of the Confucian facts is forgotten, which is the attitude we should take when studying history.

The following is considered the basic method of studying history. Under this basic method, we must find materials to carry out research. The so-called historical materials are nothing more than: 1. books that record history, 2. antiques unearthed from underground, and 3. folk songs and legends. However, in many past materials, especially in many past materials in China, many are forged, so that when Mr. Qian Xuantong studied Chinese history, he changed his name to Yigu Xuantong. When collecting materials, one must distinguish between true and false, and cannot use them randomly. In addition, there are many problems in sorting out materials and engaging in writing. But due to space limitations, I have to skip it.

Special report

Overseas Chinese in the World (10) 211

— Zhong Minyi

In addition, there are many important places in the Far East where there are many overseas Chinese, but due to various reasons, I have to skip it.

4. Overseas Chinese in Europe

Although my country has had commercial relations with European countries for a long time, until now, there are only two or three thousand overseas Chinese in the whole of Europe. The situation of overseas Chinese in various parts of Europe is described below.

France

In France, in addition to students studying abroad, there are very few pure businessmen and workers. The very few Chinese businessmen among them mostly open antique shops, hotels, restaurants and grocery stores here; their capital is also very small, so it can be said that there is no position in the business world. Li Shizeng, the current member of the Central Committee, and others once founded a tofu company in Paris when they were in France, making Chinese tofu famous in the world; but this company has now been closed, and the reason is probably the lack of managers. As for the Chinese workers in France, most of them were recruited by the French in China during the European War; many of these Chinese workers were sent back to China after the war, so the Chinese workers who are still living in France now are only sailors in Marseille and factory workers near Paris, and the number is only two or three hundred. In addition, there are about one or two thousand Chinese students scattered in Paris, Lyon and other places. However, the mobility of these students is very high, and there are increases and decreases at any time, so it is difficult to determine the number of people.

Germany

Among the overseas Chinese in Europe, Germany is the most numerous besides France. There are about six or seven hundred Chinese businessmen in Berlin and other places. In addition, there are about sixty or seventy Chinese sailors who travel between Shanghai and Berlin and do small business. As for our students studying in Germany, there are also about five or six hundred people. In total, there are only about one thousand overseas Chinese in Germany, and they are not very important in all aspects.

United Kingdom

There are only about one thousand overseas Chinese in the United Kingdom. They all live in London, Liverpool and other places. Some of them are sailors and some are workers; those in Liverpool are mostly laundry workers. Because there are very few people, they are not very important in all aspects, so the British do not pay much attention to the overseas Chinese in the UK, and at the same time, the overseas Chinese in the UK can live peacefully, although their lives are relatively poor.

Other countries

In addition to France, Germany and the United Kingdom, countries such as the Soviet Union, Belgium, the Netherlands, Switzerland, Poland, Australia, and Portugal also have traces of overseas Chinese; the most numerous among the overseas Chinese in these countries are sailors, workers and students studying abroad, but there is no accurate statistic on how many people there are now. If we talk about the number of overseas Chinese in the whole of Europe, it is about twenty to thirty thousand; among them, workers and sailors are the most numerous, followed by students, and businessmen are the least.

5. Overseas Chinese in the Americas

United States

When it comes to the Americas, of course, the United States is the representative; so we should start talking about overseas Chinese in the Americas from the United States.

Everyone knows that the United States is a capitalist country that has risen relatively late but has developed the fastest. At the beginning of the nineteenth century, when the United States was in need of labor, many Chinese workers went there. After the discovery of the California gold mine, the number of Chinese people going to the United States increased day by day. According to statistics, 1890 was the period with the largest number of overseas Chinese in the United States, reaching 107,488 people. Later, due to the competition of white people, the number of overseas Chinese in the United States gradually decreased. In addition, with the various restrictions imposed on overseas Chinese by the US government, as of now, overseas Chinese in the United States have shown no promising future. (To be continued)

Tianyi's "Sea Burial" Location Shooting Team Work Record 214

— Bai Yun

Today we are active again on the north side of Shidao.

Fu Baolu pushed the small cart and followed the fishermen into the city. The fishermen on the island were all unreasonable. Director Wang kindly explained to them, but they always seemed to be uncontrollable, so it took a lot of time to shoot this great scene.

On the road of the Yagang, Tian Fang pushed the cart, Xiao Fu supported it, and Xiao Chen pulled the rope in front. The three were covered in sweat and it was very hard. Under the tense atmosphere, Xiao Chen was still eating his big cake. Tian Fang was panting, and his facial expression seemed even more gloomy. Baolu's movements were powerful everywhere, which was really beautiful.

Fang Pei, a girl with pigtails, and her neighbor, Li Ying, walked barefoot, exposing their thighs and squatting on the reefs on the beach to pick up aphids? From the distant waves, the floating corpses of dead people vaguely appeared. Li Ying suddenly had an inspiration and thought of her husband who had not returned from fishing. She stared blankly at the sky and secretly prayed: "Dragon King, please bless my husband!" But the floating corpse on the sea turned out to be her husband. She changed her attitude and cried wildly.

Innocent and lovely Fang Pei, she didn't seem to have anything at all, and she wouldn't comfort her sister.

The work of this location shooting was extremely difficult, which made everyone working very worried. The crabs on the stone reefs were as sharp as knives. They who worked in the water all had bleeding wounds. Director Wang was a man of ten, so his wounds were more than others. Old Jiang Wei Pengfei went to the sea wearing his pants, and cameraman Shen Yongshi also struggled with the sea regardless of his life.

Chen Juanjuan, who will star in "The Lost Lamb" 215

— Du Ao photo

Anecdotes of "The Tempest" 216

— Qing Yun

"The Tempest" contains: "The Tempest of Life", the tempest of society, and the "Tempest" of the times.

"The Tempest" reveals the gloomy facts in the tempest era, and provides a way for people to struggle in the tempest era!

There is no decadent song, only the sound that stirs your emotions and represents your cry.

Here are the symphonies of cannons and guns that are demonstrating to us, and the ice cream of thick thighs and breasts that are anesthetizing us!

"The Tempest" is full of the elements necessary for stimulation, tension and moving art.

"The Tempest" has new faces and new techniques.

The main theme of "The Tempest" is: fighting for the country and bleeding for justice!

In "The Tempest" there is at the same time: a sweet song and dance is played on one side, and a realistic tragicomedy of the survival of the fittest is played on the other.

"The Tempest" is Mr. Yuan Nongmei's work on the road to success!
